\NormalFont\ShortTitle{Psalms}
{\MT Psalm
\par }{\SH \par }{\MS Book 1 \newline  (Psalms 1-41)Psalm 1

\par }\PsalmChap{1}{\PP \par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}How blessed
is the one
who does not
follow
the advice
of the wicked,
\par }{\Q or stand
in
the pathway
with sinners,
\par }{\Q or
sit in
the assembly of scoffers!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Instead
he finds pleasure
in obeying
the
{\ND{Lord}}’s
commands;

\par }{\Q he meditates
on his commands day
and night.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}He is like
a tree
planted
by flowing
streams;
\par }{\Q it yields
its fruit
at the proper time,
\par }{\Q and its
leaves
never
fall off.

\par }{\Q He succeeds
in everything
he attempts.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Not
so
with the wicked!
\par }{\Q Instead
they are like wind-driven
chaff.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}For this reason
the wicked
cannot
withstand
judgment,
\par }{\Q nor can sinners
join the assembly
of the godly.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Certainly
the {\ND{Lord}}
guards
the way
of the godly,
\par }{\Q but the way
of the wicked
ends in destruction.

\par }\PsalmChap{2}{\PP \par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Why
do the nations
rebel?

\par }{\Q Why are the countries
devising
plots that will fail?
\par }{\Q \VS{2}The kings
of the earth
form a united
front;

\par }{\Q the rulers
collaborate
\par }{\Q against
the {\ND{Lord}}
and his anointed king.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}They say, “Let’s tear
off the shackles
they’ve
put
on us!

\par }{\Q Let’s
free ourselves from
their ropes!”
\par }{\Q \VS{4}The one enthroned in
heaven
laughs
in disgust;

\par }{\Q the Lord
taunts them.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Then
he angrily
speaks
to
them
\par }{\Q and terrifies
them in his rage, saying,
\par }{\Q \VS{6}“I myself
have installed
my king
\par }{\Q on
Zion,
my holy
hill.”
\par }{\Q \VS{7}The king
says, “I will announce
the
{\ND{Lord’s}}
decree.
He said
to me:

\par }{\Q ‘You
are my son! This very day
I
have become your father!
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Ask
me,
\par }{\Q and I will give
you the nations
as your inheritance,
\par }{\Q the ends
of the earth
as your personal property.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}You will break
them with an iron
scepter;
\par }{\Q you will smash
them like a potter’s
jar!’ ”
\par }{\Q \VS{10}So now,
you kings,
do what is wise;
\par }{\Q you rulers
of the earth,
submit to correction!
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Serve
the {\ND{Lord}}
in fear!
\par }{\Q Repent
in terror!
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Give sincere homage!

\par }{\Q Otherwise
he will be angry,
\par }{\Q and you will die
because
of your behavior,
\par }{\Q when his anger
quickly
ignites.
\par }{\Q How blessed
are all
who take shelter in him!


\par }\PsalmChap{3}{\D 
A psalm
of David,
written when he fled
from his son
Absalom.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}{\ND{Lord}}, how
numerous
are my enemies!
\par }{\Q Many
attack me.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Many
say
about me,
\par }{\Q “God
will not
deliver
him.” (Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{3}But you,

{\ND{Lord}}, are a shield
that protects me;
\par }{\Q you are my glory
and the one who restores me.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}To
the
{\ND{Lord}}
I cried
out,

\par }{\Q and he answered
me from his holy
hill.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{5}I
rested
and slept;
\par }{\Q I awoke,
for
the {\ND{Lord}}
protects me.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I am not
afraid
of the multitude
of people
\par }{\Q who attack me from all directions.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Rise up,

{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q Deliver
me, my God!
\par }{\Q Yes,
you will strike
all
my enemies
on the jaw;
\par }{\Q you will break
the teeth
of the wicked.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}The
{\ND{Lord}}
delivers;
\par }{\Q you show favor
to your people.
(Selah)


\par }\PsalmChap{4}{\D 
For the music director,
to be accompanied by stringed instruments;
a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}When I call
out, answer
me,
\par }{\Q O God
who vindicates me!

\par }{\Q Though I am hemmed
in, you will lead me into a wide, open place.

\par }{\Q Have mercy
on me and respond
to my prayer!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}You men,
how
long will you try to turn my honor
into shame?

\par }{\Q How long will you love
what is worthless
\par }{\Q and search
for what is deceptive? (Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Realize
that
the {\ND{Lord}}
shows
the godly
special favor;

\par }{\Q the {\ND{Lord}}
responds when
I cry
out to him.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Tremble
with fear and do not
sin!

\par }{\Q Meditate
as you lie in bed,
and repent
of your ways! (Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Offer
the prescribed
sacrifices
\par }{\Q and trust
in the
{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Many
say,
“Who can
show
us anything good?”
\par }{\Q Smile
upon us,
{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q \VS{7}You make
me happier
\par }{\Q than those who have abundant
grain
and wine.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}I will lie
down and sleep
peacefully,
\par }{\Q for
you,

{\ND{Lord}}, make me safe
and secure.


\par }\PsalmChap{5}{\D 
For the music director,
to
be accompanied by wind instruments;
a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Listen
to what I say,

{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q Carefully consider
my complaint!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Pay attention
to my cry
for help,
\par }{\Q my king
and my God,
\par }{\Q for
I am praying
to you!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}{\ND{Lord}}, in the morning
you will hear
me;

\par }{\Q in the morning
I will present
my case
to you and then wait expectantly for an answer.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Certainly
you are not
a God
who approves
of evil;
\par }{\Q evil people
cannot
dwell
with you.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Arrogant people
cannot
stand
in your presence;
\par }{\Q you hate
all
who behave
wickedly.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}You destroy
liars;
\par }{\Q the {\ND{Lord}}
despises
violent
and deceitful
people.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}But as for me,
because of your great
faithfulness
I will enter
your house;
\par }{\Q I will bow
down toward
your holy
temple
as I worship you.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}{\ND{Lord}}, lead
me in your righteousness
\par }{\Q because
of those who wait to ambush
me,

\par }{\Q remove the obstacles
in the way in which you are guiding me!
\par }{\Q \VS{9}For
they do
not
speak
the truth;

\par }{\Q their stomachs
are like the place of destruction,

\par }{\Q their throats
like an open
grave,
\par }{\Q their tongues
like a steep slope leading into it.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Condemn
them, O God!
\par }{\Q May their own schemes
be their downfall!

\par }{\Q Drive
them away
because of their many
acts of insurrection,
\par }{\Q for
they have rebelled against you.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}But may all
who take shelter
in you be happy!

\par }{\Q May they continually
shout
for joy!

\par }{\Q Shelter
them so that those who are loyal
to you
may rejoice!
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Certainly
you
reward
the godly,

{\ND{Lord}}.
\par }{\Q Like a shield
you protect
them in your good favor.


\par }\PsalmChap{6}{\D 
For the music director,
to be accompanied by stringed instruments,
according to the
{\IT{
sheminith}}
style; a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}{\ND{Lord}}, do not
rebuke
me in your anger!
\par }{\Q Do not
discipline
me in your raging fury!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Have mercy
on me,
{\ND{Lord}}, for
I am
frail!
\par }{\Q Heal
me,
{\ND{Lord}}, for
my bones
are shaking!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}I am absolutely
terrified,
\par }{\Q and you,

{\ND{Lord}} –
how long will this continue?
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Relent,

{\ND{Lord}}, rescue
me!

\par }{\Q Deliver
me because
of your faithfulness!
\par }{\Q \VS{5}For
no
one remembers you in the realm
of death,

\par }{\Q In Sheol
who
gives you thanks?
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I am exhausted
as I groan;
\par }{\Q all
night
long I drench
my bed
in tears;

\par }{\Q my tears
saturate
the cushion
beneath me.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}My eyes
grow dim
from suffering;
\par }{\Q they grow
weak because of all
my enemies.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Turn
back from me,
all
you who behave
wickedly,
\par }{\Q for
the {\ND{Lord}}
has heard
the sound
of my weeping!
\par }{\Q \VS{9}The
{\ND{Lord}}
has heard
my appeal for mercy;
\par }{\Q the {\ND{Lord}}
has accepted
my prayer.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}May all
my enemies
be humiliated
and absolutely terrified!

\par }{\Q May they turn back
and be suddenly
humiliated!


\par }\PsalmChap{7}{\D 
A musical composition
by David,
which
he sang
to the
{\ND{Lord}}
concerning
a Benjaminite
named Cush.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O
{\ND{Lord}}
my God,
in you I have taken shelter.
\par }{\Q Deliver
me from all
who chase
me! Rescue me!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Otherwise
they will rip
me
to shreds
like a lion;
\par }{\Q they will tear
me to bits
and no one
will be able to rescue me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}O
{\ND{Lord}}
my God,
if
I have done
what they say,

\par }{\Q or
am guilty
of unjust actions,
\par }{\Q \VS{4}or
have wronged
my ally,
\par }{\Q or helped
his lawless
enemy,
\par }{\Q \VS{5}may an enemy
relentlessly
chase
me and catch
me;

\par }{\Q may he trample
me to death

\par }{\Q and leave me lying dishonored
in the dust.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Stand
up angrily,

{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q Rise
up with raging fury
against my enemies!

\par }{\Q Wake
up for my sake and execute
the judgment
you have decreed for them!
\par }{\Q \VS{7}The countries
are assembled
all around
you;

\par }{\Q take once
more your rightful place over them!
\par }{\Q \VS{8}The
{\ND{Lord}}
judges
the nations.
\par }{\Q Vindicate
me,
{\ND{Lord}}, because I am innocent,
\par }{\Q because I am blameless, O Exalted One!
\par }{\Q \VS{9}May
the evil deeds
of the wicked
come to an end!

\par }{\Q But make the innocent
secure,
\par }{\Q O righteous
God,
\par }{\Q you who examine
inner thoughts
and motives!
\par }{\Q \VS{10}The Exalted God
is my
shield,
\par }{\Q the one who delivers
the morally
upright.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}God
is a just
judge;
\par }{\Q he
is
angry
throughout
the day.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}If
a person does not
repent,
God sharpens his sword
\par }{\Q and prepares
to shoot his bow.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}He prepares
to use deadly
weapons
against him;

\par }{\Q he gets
ready to shoot flaming
arrows.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}See
the one who is pregnant
with wickedness,
\par }{\Q who conceives
destructive plans,
\par }{\Q and gives birth
to harmful
lies –

\par }{\Q \VS{15}he digs
a pit
\par }{\Q and then falls
into the hole
he has made.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}He becomes
the victim
of his own destructive plans
\par }{\Q and the violence
he intended for others falls
on
his own head.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}I will thank
the {\ND{Lord}}
for his justice;
\par }{\Q I will sing praises
to the sovereign

{\ND{Lord}}!


\par }\PsalmChap{8}{\D 
For the music director,
according
{\IT{to the
gittith}} style;
a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O
{\ND{Lord}},
our Lord,
\par }{\Q how
magnificent
is your reputation
throughout
the earth!
\par }{\Q You
reveal your majesty
in the heavens
above!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}From the mouths
of children
and nursing
babies
\par }{\Q you have ordained
praise on account of your
adversaries,
\par }{\Q so that you might
put an end
to the vindictive
enemy.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}When
I look
up at the heavens,
which your fingers
made,
\par }{\Q and see the moon
and the stars,
which
you set
in place,
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Of what
importance is the human
race, that
you should notice
them?
\par }{\Q Of what importance is mankind,
that
you should pay attention to them,
\par }{\Q \VS{5}and make them a little
less
than the heavenly
beings?

\par }{\Q You grant mankind
honor
and majesty;
\par }{\Q \VS{6}you appoint them to rule
over your
creation;
\par }{\Q you have placed
everything
under
their
authority,
\par }{\Q \VS{7}including all
the sheep
and cattle,
\par }{\Q as well
as the wild
animals,
\par }{\Q \VS{8}the birds
in the sky,
the fish
in the sea
\par }{\Q and everything that moves through
the currents
of the seas.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}O
{\ND{Lord}}, our Lord,
\par }{\Q how
magnificent
is your reputation
throughout
the earth!


\par }\PsalmChap{9}{\D 
For the music director;
{\IT{according to the
alumoth-labben}}
style; a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}I will thank
the {\ND{Lord}}
with all
my heart!
\par }{\Q I will tell
about all
your amazing deeds!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I will be happy
and rejoice
in you!
\par }{\Q I will sing praises
to you, O sovereign
One!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}When my enemies
turn
back,
\par }{\Q they trip
and are defeated
before you.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For
you defended
my just
cause;
\par }{\Q from your throne
you pronounced
a just decision.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}You terrified
the nations
with your battle cry;

\par }{\Q you destroyed
the wicked;
\par }{\Q you permanently
wiped out
all memory of them.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}The enemy’s
cities have been reduced
to permanent
ruins;
\par }{\Q you destroyed
their cities;
\par }{\Q all memory
of the enemies
has perished.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}But the
{\ND{Lord}}
rules forever;
\par }{\Q he reigns
in
a just manner.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}He judges
the world
fairly;
\par }{\Q he
makes just legal
decisions
for the nations.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Consequently
the {\ND{Lord}}
provides
safety
for the oppressed;

\par }{\Q he provides
safety in times
of trouble.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Your loyal followers trust
in you,
\par }{\Q for
you,
{\ND{Lord}}, do not
abandon
those who seek your help.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Sing praises
to the
{\ND{Lord}}, who rules
in Zion!
\par }{\Q Tell
the nations
what he has done!
\par }{\Q \VS{12}For
the one
who takes revenge
against murderers
took notice
of the oppressed;
\par }{\Q he did not
overlook
their cry for help
\par }{\Q \VS{13}when they prayed:

\par }{\Q “Have mercy
on me,
{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q See
how I am oppressed
by those who hate
me,

\par }{\Q O one who can snatch
me away
from the gates
of death!
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Then
I will
tell
about all
your praiseworthy
acts;

\par }{\Q in the gates
of Daughter
Zion
I will rejoice
because of your deliverance.”
\par }{\Q \VS{15}The nations
fell
into the pit
they had made;
\par }{\Q their feet
were caught
in the net
they had hidden.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}The
{\ND{Lord}}
revealed
himself;
\par }{\Q he accomplished
justice;
\par }{\Q the wicked
were ensnared
by their own actions. (Higgaion.
Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{17}The wicked
are turned back
and sent to Sheol;
\par }{\Q this is the destiny of all
the nations
that ignore
God,
\par }{\Q \VS{18}for
the needy
are not
permanently
ignored,
\par }{\Q the hopes
of the oppressed
are not forever
dashed.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Rise
up,
{\ND{Lord}}!

\par }{\Q Don’t
let men
be defiant!

\par }{\Q May
the nations
be judged
in your presence!
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Terrify
them,
{\ND{Lord}}!

\par }{\Q Let the nations
know
they
are
mere
mortals! (Selah)


\par }\PsalmChap{10}{\PP \par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Why,

{\ND{Lord}}, do you stand
far
off?
\par }{\Q Why do you pay no attention during
times
of trouble?
\par }{\Q \VS{2}The wicked
arrogantly
chase
the oppressed;
\par }{\Q the oppressed are trapped
by the schemes
the wicked
have dreamed up.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Yes,
the wicked
man boasts because he gets
what he wants;
\par }{\Q the one who robs
others curses
and rejects
the {\ND{Lord}}.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}The wicked
man is so arrogant
he always thinks,
\par }{\Q “God
won’t
hold me accountable;
he doesn’t care.”
\par }{\Q \VS{5}He is secure at all
times.
\par }{\Q He has no regard for your commands;

\par }{\Q he disdains
all
his enemies.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}He says
to himself,
\par }{\Q “I will never be upended,
\par }{\Q because I experience
no
calamity.”
\par }{\Q \VS{7}His mouth
is full
of curses
and deceptive,
harmful words;
\par }{\Q his tongue
injures
and destroys.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}He waits
in ambush
near the villages;
\par }{\Q in hidden places
he kills
the innocent.
\par }{\Q His eyes
look for
some unfortunate victim.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}He lies in ambush
in a hidden place,
like a lion
in a thicket;
\par }{\Q he lies in ambush,
waiting to catch
the oppressed;
\par }{\Q he catches
the oppressed
by pulling
in his net.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}His victims
are crushed
and beaten down;
\par }{\Q they are trapped
in his sturdy nets.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}He says
to himself,
\par }{\Q “God
overlooks
it;
\par }{\Q he does not
pay attention;
\par }{\Q he never notices.”
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Rise
up,
{\ND{Lord}}!

\par }{\Q O God,
strike
him down!

\par }{\Q Do not
forget
the oppressed!
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Why
does the wicked
man reject
God?

\par }{\Q He says
to himself, “You will not
hold me accountable.”
\par }{\Q \VS{14}You have taken notice,
\par }{\Q for
you
always see
one who inflicts
pain
and suffering.
\par }{\Q The unfortunate victim
entrusts
his cause
to
you;

\par }{\Q you
deliver
the fatherless.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Break
the arm
of the wicked
and evil
man!
\par }{\Q Hold him accountable
for his wicked
deeds,

\par }{\Q which he thought you would not discover.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}The
{\ND{Lord}}
rules
forever!

\par }{\Q The nations
are driven out
of his land.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}{\ND{Lord}}, you have heard
the request
of the oppressed;
\par }{\Q you make them feel secure
because you listen to their prayer.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}You defend
the fatherless
and oppressed,

\par }{\Q so that mere mortals
may
no longer
terrorize them.


\par }\PsalmChap{11}{\D 
For the music director;
by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}In the
{\ND{Lord}}
I have taken shelter.
\par }{\Q How
can you say
to me,
\par }{\Q “Flee
to a mountain
like a bird!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}For
look,
the wicked
prepare their
bows,
\par }{\Q they put
their arrows
on
the strings,
\par }{\Q to shoot
in the darkness
at the morally
upright.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}When
the foundations
are destroyed,
\par }{\Q what can
the godly
accomplish?”
\par }{\Q \VS{4}The
{\ND{Lord}}
is in his holy
temple;
\par }{\Q the
{\ND{Lord}}’s
throne
is in heaven.
\par }{\Q His eyes
watch;
\par }{\Q his eyes
examine
all people.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}The
{\ND{Lord}}
approves
of the godly,
\par }{\Q but he hates
the wicked
and those who love
to do violence.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}May the
{\ND{Lord}} rain down
burning coals
and brimstone
on
the wicked!
\par }{\Q A whirlwind is what they deserve!
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Certainly
the {\ND{Lord}}
is just;

\par }{\Q he rewards
godly deeds;
\par }{\Q the upright
will experience his favor.


\par }\PsalmChap{12}{\D 
For the music director;
according
{\IT{to the
sheminith}}
style; a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Deliver,

{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q For
the godly
have disappeared;
\par }{\Q people
of integrity
have vanished.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}People lie
to one
another;
\par }{\Q they flatter
and deceive.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}May the
{\ND{Lord}}
cut off
all
flattering
lips,
\par }{\Q and the tongue
that boasts!
\par }{\Q \VS{4}They say, “We speak
persuasively;
\par }{\Q we know how to flatter and boast.
\par }{\Q Who
is our master?”
\par }{\Q \VS{5}“Because of the violence
done to the oppressed,
\par }{\Q because of the painful
cries of the needy,
\par }{\Q I will spring into action,”
says
the {\ND{Lord}}.
\par }{\Q “I will provide
the safety
they so desperately desire.”
\par }{\Q \VS{6}The
{\ND{Lord}}’s
words
are absolutely reliable.
\par }{\Q They are as untainted
as silver
purified
in a furnace
on the ground,
\par }{\Q where it is thoroughly
refined.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}You,

{\ND{Lord}}, will protect
them;

\par }{\Q you will continually
shelter
each one from
these evil people,
\par }{\Q \VS{8}for the wicked
seem to be everywhere,
\par }{\Q when people
promote
evil.


\par }\PsalmChap{13}{\D 
For the music director;
a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}How long,

{\ND{Lord}}, will you continue
to
ignore
me?

\par }{\Q How long will you pay no attention to me?
\par }{\Q \VS{2}How
long
must I worry,
\par }{\Q and suffer
in broad daylight?

\par }{\Q How
long
will my enemy
gloat
over me?
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Look
at me! Answer
me, O
{\ND{Lord}}
my God!
\par }{\Q Revive
me,
or
else I will die!
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Then my enemy
will say, “I have defeated
him!”
\par }{\Q Then my foes
will rejoice
because
I am
upended.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}But I
trust
in your faithfulness.
\par }{\Q May I rejoice
because of your deliverance!
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I will sing
praises to the
{\ND{Lord}}
\par }{\Q when
he vindicates me.


\par }\PsalmChap{14}{\D 
For the music director;
by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Fools
say
to themselves, “There is no
God.”
\par }{\Q They sin and commit
evil deeds;
\par }{\Q none
of them does what
is right.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}The
{\ND{Lord}}
looks
down from heaven
at the human
race,

\par }{\Q to see
if there is anyone
who is wise
and seeks
God.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Everyone
rejects
God;

\par }{\Q they are all
morally corrupt.
\par }{\Q None
of them does
what is right,
\par }{\Q not
even
one!
\par }{\Q \VS{4}All
those who behave
wickedly
do not
understand –

\par }{\Q those who devour my people as if they were eating bread,
\par }{\Q and do not call out to the
{\ND{Lord}}.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They are absolutely
terrified,
\par }{\Q for
God
defends
the godly.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}You want to humiliate
the oppressed,
\par }{\Q even though
the {\ND{Lord}}
is their shelter.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}I wish
the deliverance
of Israel
would come from Zion!
\par }{\Q When the
{\ND{Lord}}
restores the well-being
of his people,
\par }{\Q may
Jacob
rejoice,
\par }{\Q may Israel
be happy!


\par }\PsalmChap{15}{\D 
A psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}{\ND{Lord}}, who
may be a guest
in your home?

\par }{\Q Who
may live
on your holy
hill?
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Whoever lives
a blameless
life,

\par }{\Q does what
is right,
\par }{\Q and speaks
honestly.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}He does not
slander,
\par }{\Q or
do
harm
to others,

\par }{\Q or
insult
his neighbor.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}He despises
a reprobate,
\par }{\Q but honors
the
{\ND{Lord}}’s
loyal followers.
\par }{\Q He makes firm commitments
and does not
renege
on his promise.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}He does not
charge
interest
when he lends his money.
\par }{\Q He does not
take
bribes
to testify against
the innocent.
\par }{\Q The one who lives
like this
will never
be upended.


\par }\PsalmChap{16}{\D 
A prayer
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Protect
me, O God,
for
I have taken shelter in you.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I say
to the
{\ND{Lord}}, “You are the Lord,
\par }{\Q my only source of well-being.”
\par }{\Q \VS{3}As
for God’s chosen people
who are
in the land,
\par }{\Q and the leading officials
I admired so much –
\par }{\Q \VS{4}their troubles
multiply,
\par }{\Q they desire
other
gods.

\par }{\Q I will not
pour out
drink offerings
of blood
to their gods,

\par }{\Q nor
will I make vows
in the name
of their gods.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}{\ND{Lord}}, you give me stability
and prosperity;
\par }{\Q you
make
my future secure.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}It is
as
if I have been given fertile fields
\par }{\Q or received a beautiful tract
of land.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}I will praise
the {\ND{Lord}}
who
guides
me;
\par }{\Q yes,
during the night
I reflect
and learn.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}I constantly
trust
in the
{\ND{Lord}};

\par }{\Q because
he is at my right hand,
I will not
be upended.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}So
my heart
rejoices
\par }{\Q and I am happy;
\par }{\Q My
life is safe.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}You will not
abandon
me
to Sheol;
\par }{\Q you will not
allow
your faithful follower
to see
the Pit.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}You lead
me in the path
of life;
\par }{\Q I experience absolute
joy
in your presence;
\par }{\Q you always give me sheer delight.


\par }\PsalmChap{17}{\D 
A prayer
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}{\ND{Lord}}, consider
my just cause!

\par }{\Q Pay attention
to my cry for help!
\par }{\Q Listen
to the prayer
\par }{\Q I sincerely
offer!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Make
a just decision
on my behalf!

\par }{\Q Decide what is right!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}You have scrutinized
my inner motives;
\par }{\Q you have examined
me during the night.
\par }{\Q You have carefully evaluated
me, but you find
no
sin.
\par }{\Q I am determined
I will say
nothing sinful.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}As for the actions
of people –
\par }{\Q just as you have commanded,
\par }{\Q I
have not followed
in the footsteps
of violent men.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}I
carefully obey your commands;

\par }{\Q I do not
deviate from them.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I
call
to you for
you will answer
me, O God.
\par }{\Q Listen
to me!

\par }{\Q Hear
what I say!
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Accomplish awesome,
faithful
deeds,

\par }{\Q you who powerfully
deliver
those who look to you for protection from their enemies.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Protect me as you would protect
the pupil
of your eye!

\par }{\Q Hide
me in the shadow
of your wings!
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Protect me from
the wicked
men who
attack
me,
\par }{\Q my enemies
who crowd around me for the kill.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}They are calloused;
\par }{\Q they speak
arrogantly.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}They attack
me, now
they surround
me;

\par }{\Q they intend
to throw
me to the ground.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}He is like
a lion
that wants to tear
its prey to bits,

\par }{\Q like a young lion
crouching
in hidden places.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Rise
up,
{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q Confront
him! Knock
him down!

\par }{\Q Use your sword
to rescue
me
from the wicked man!
\par }{\Q \VS{14}{\ND{Lord}}, use your power
to deliver me from these murderers,
\par }{\Q from the murderers
of this world!

\par }{\Q They enjoy prosperity;
\par }{\Q you overwhelm
them with the riches
they desire.

\par }{\Q They have many
children,
\par }{\Q and leave
their wealth
to their offspring.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}As for me, because I
am innocent
I will see
your face;
\par }{\Q when I awake you will reveal yourself to me.


\par }\PsalmChap{18}{\D 
For the music director;
by the
{\ND{Lord}}’s
servant
David,
who
sang
to the
{\ND{Lord}}
the
words
of this
song
when
the {\ND{Lord}}
rescued
him from the power
of all
his enemies,
including Saul.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}He said:

\par }{\Q “I love
you,
{\ND{Lord}}, my source of strength!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}The
{\ND{Lord}}
is my high ridge,
my stronghold,
my deliverer.
\par }{\Q My God
is my rocky
summit where I take shelter,
\par }{\Q my shield,
the horn
that saves
me, and my refuge.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}I called
to the
{\ND{Lord}}, who is worthy of praise,
\par }{\Q and I was delivered
from
my enemies.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}The waves
of death
engulfed
me,
\par }{\Q the currents
of chaos
overwhelmed me.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}The ropes
of Sheol
tightened
around
me,

\par }{\Q the snares
of death trapped me.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}In my distress
I called
to the
{\ND{Lord}};
\par }{\Q I cried out
to
my God.
\par }{\Q From his heavenly temple
he heard
my voice;
\par }{\Q he listened to my cry
for help.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}The earth
heaved
and shook;
\par }{\Q the roots
of the mountains
trembled;
\par }{\Q they heaved
because
he was angry.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Smoke
ascended
from his nose;
\par }{\Q fire
devoured
as it came from
his mouth;
\par }{\Q he hurled down fiery coals.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}He made
the sky
sink
as he descended;
\par }{\Q a thick cloud
was under
his feet.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}He mounted
a winged
angel and flew;
\par }{\Q he glided
on
the wings
of the wind.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}He shrouded
himself in darkness,
\par }{\Q in thick
rain
clouds.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}From the brightness
in front
of him came
\par }{\Q hail
and fiery
coals.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}The
{\ND{Lord}}
thundered
in the sky;
\par }{\Q the sovereign
One shouted.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}He shot
his arrows
and scattered
them,

\par }{\Q many
lightning
bolts
and routed them.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}The depths
of the sea were exposed;
\par }{\Q the inner regions
of the world
were uncovered
\par }{\Q by
your battle cry,

{\ND{Lord}},
\par }{\Q by
the powerful breath
from your nose.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}He reached
down from above
and took
hold of me;
\par }{\Q he pulled
me from the surging
water.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}He rescued me from my strong
enemy,
\par }{\Q from those who hate
me,
\par }{\Q for
they were too
strong for me.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}They confronted
me in my day
of calamity,
\par }{\Q but the
{\ND{Lord}}
helped me.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}He brought
me out
into a wide open place;
\par }{\Q he delivered
me because
he was pleased with me.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}The
{\ND{Lord}}
repaid
me for my godly
deeds;

\par }{\Q he rewarded
my blameless
behavior.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}For
I have obeyed
the
{\ND{Lord}}’s
commands;
\par }{\Q I have not
rebelled
against my God.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}For
I am aware
of all
his regulations,
\par }{\Q and I do not
reject
his rules.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}I was
innocent
before him,
\par }{\Q and kept
myself from sinning.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}The
{\ND{Lord}}
rewarded
me for my godly
deeds;

\par }{\Q he took notice of my blameless
behavior.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}You prove
to be loyal
to one who is faithful;
\par }{\Q you prove
to be trustworthy
to one who is
innocent.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}You prove
to be
reliable to
one who is blameless,
\par }{\Q but
you prove to be deceptive
to one who is perverse.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}For
you
deliver
oppressed
people,
\par }{\Q but you bring down those who have a proud look.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}Indeed,
you
are my lamp,

{\ND{Lord}}.

\par }{\Q My God
illuminates
the darkness around me.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}Indeed,
with your help I can charge against an army;
\par }{\Q by my God’s
power I can jump over
a wall.
\par }{\Q \VS{30}The one true God
acts in a faithful manner;
\par }{\Q the
{\ND{Lord}}’s
promise
is reliable;
\par }{\Q he is
a shield
to all
who take shelter in him.
\par }{\Q \VS{31}Indeed,
who
is God
besides
the {\ND{Lord}}?
\par }{\Q Who
is a protector
besides
our God?
\par }{\Q \VS{32}The one true God
gives
me strength;
\par }{\Q he removes
the obstacles
in my way.
\par }{\Q \VS{33}He gives me the agility
of a deer;
\par }{\Q he enables me to negotiate
the rugged terrain.
\par }{\Q \VS{34}He trains
my hands
for battle;
\par }{\Q my arms can bend
even the strongest
bow.
\par }{\Q \VS{35}You give
me your protective
shield;
\par }{\Q your right hand
supports
me;

\par }{\Q your willingness
to help enables me to prevail.
\par }{\Q \VS{36}You widen
my path;
\par }{\Q my feet
do not
slip.
\par }{\Q \VS{37}I chase
my enemies
and catch
them;
\par }{\Q I do not
turn back
until
I wipe them out.
\par }{\Q \VS{38}I beat
them to death;

\par }{\Q they fall
at my feet.
\par }{\Q \VS{39}You give
me strength
for battle;
\par }{\Q you make my foes kneel
before me.
\par }{\Q \VS{40}You make
my enemies
retreat;
\par }{\Q I destroy
those who hate
me.
\par }{\Q \VS{41}They cry out,
but there is no
one to help
them;

\par }{\Q they cry out to the
{\ND{Lord}}, but he does not
answer them.
\par }{\Q \VS{42}I grind
them as fine windblown dust;
\par }{\Q I beat them underfoot
like clay
in the streets.
\par }{\Q \VS{43}You rescue
me from a hostile
army;
\par }{\Q you make
me a
leader
of nations;
\par }{\Q people
over whom I had no
authority are now my subjects.
\par }{\Q \VS{44}When they hear
of my exploits, they submit
to me.

\par }{\Q Foreigners
are powerless before me;
\par }{\Q \VS{45}foreigners
lose their courage;
\par }{\Q they shake with fear as
they leave their
strongholds.
\par }{\Q \VS{46}The
{\ND{Lord}}
is alive!

\par }{\Q My protector
is praiseworthy!

\par }{\Q The God
who delivers
me is exalted as king!
\par }{\Q \VS{47}The one true God
completely vindicates
me;

\par }{\Q he makes
nations
submit to me.
\par }{\Q \VS{48}He delivers
me from my enemies;
\par }{\Q you snatch
me away from those who attack me;

\par }{\Q you rescue
me from violent
men.
\par }{\Q \VS{49}So
I will give you thanks
before the nations,
O
{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q I will sing praises
to you!
\par }{\Q \VS{50}He gives
his chosen king
magnificent
victories;
\par }{\Q he
is faithful
to his chosen ruler,
\par }{\Q to David
and his descendants
forever.”


\par }\PsalmChap{19}{\D 
For the music director;
a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}The heavens
declare
the glory
of God;
\par }{\Q the sky displays his handiwork.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Day
after day
it speaks out;
\par }{\Q night
after night
it reveals
his greatness.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}There is no
actual speech
or word,
\par }{\Q nor is its voice
literally
heard.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Yet its voice echoes
throughout
the earth;
\par }{\Q its words
carry to the distant horizon.
\par }{\Q In the sky he has pitched
a tent
for the sun.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Like a bridegroom
it emerges
from its chamber;
\par }{\Q like a strong man it enjoys
running
its course.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}It emerges
from the distant horizon,
\par }{\Q and goes from one end
of the sky
to the other;
\par }{\Q nothing
can escape
its heat.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}The law
of the {\ND{Lord}}
is perfect
\par }{\Q and preserves
one’s life.
\par }{\Q The rules
set down by the
{\ND{Lord}}
are reliable
\par }{\Q and impart wisdom
to the inexperienced.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}The
{\ND{Lord}}’s
precepts
are fair
\par }{\Q and make one joyful.
\par }{\Q The
{\ND{Lord}}’s
commands
are pure
\par }{\Q and give insight
for life.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}The commands to fear
the {\ND{Lord}}
are right
\par }{\Q and endure
forever.
\par }{\Q The judgments
given by the
{\ND{Lord}}
are trustworthy
\par }{\Q and absolutely
just.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}They are of greater value
than gold,
\par }{\Q than even a great
amount of pure gold;
\par }{\Q they bring greater delight than honey,
\par }{\Q than even the sweetest
honey
from a honeycomb.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Yes,
your servant
finds moral
guidance there;

\par }{\Q those who obey
them receive a rich
reward.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Who
can know
all his errors?

\par }{\Q Please do not punish
me for sins I am unaware of.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Moreover,
keep
me
from committing flagrant sins;
\par }{\Q do not
allow such sins to control
me.

\par }{\Q Then
I will be blameless,
\par }{\Q and innocent
of blatant
rebellion.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}May
my words
and my
thoughts
\par }{\Q be acceptable
in your sight,
\par }{\Q O
{\ND{Lord}}, my sheltering rock
and my redeemer.

(Selah)

\par }{\Q and you have granted

\par }{\Q you give him majestic

\par }{\Q \VS{6}For

\par }{\Q you give him great joy

\par }{\Q \VS{7}For

{\ND{Lord}},

{\SC{
Lord}}’s faithfulness

\par }{\Q the {\ND{Lord}}

\par }{\Q their descendants

\par }{\Q they dream up

\par }\PsalmChap{22}{\D 
For the music director;
according to the tune “Morning Doe;”
a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}My God,
my God,
why
have you abandoned
me?

\par }{\Q I groan
in prayer, but help seems
far away.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}My God,
I cry out
during the day,
\par }{\Q but you do not
answer,
\par }{\Q and during the night
my prayers
do not let up.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}You
are holy;
\par }{\Q you sit
as king receiving the praises
of Israel.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}In you our ancestors
trusted;
\par }{\Q they trusted
in you and you rescued them.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}To
you they cried
out, and they were saved;
\par }{\Q in you they trusted
and they were not
disappointed.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}But I
am a worm,
not
a man;
\par }{\Q people
insult
me and despise me.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}All
who see
me taunt
me;
\par }{\Q they mock
me and shake
their heads.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}They say,

\par }{\Q “Commit
yourself to
the {\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q Let the
{\ND{Lord}} rescue
him!
\par }{\Q Let the
{\ND{Lord}} deliver
him, for
he delights in him.”
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Yes,
you
are the one who brought me out from the womb
\par }{\Q and made me feel
secure
on
my mother’s
breasts.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}I have been dependent on you since birth;
\par }{\Q from
the time I came out
of my mother’s
womb
you
have been my God.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Do not
remain far
away from
me,
\par }{\Q for
trouble
is near
and I have no
one to help me.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Many
bulls
surround
me;
\par }{\Q powerful bulls
of Bashan
hem me in.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}They open
their mouths
to devour me

\par }{\Q like a roaring
lion
that rips its prey.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}My strength drains
away like water;
\par }{\Q all
my bones
are dislocated;
\par }{\Q my heart
is like wax;
\par }{\Q it melts away
inside me.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}The roof of my mouth is as dry
as a piece of pottery;
\par }{\Q my tongue
sticks
to my gums.
\par }{\Q You set
me in the dust
of death.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Yes,
wild dogs
surround me –
\par }{\Q a gang of evil men crowd around me;
\par }{\Q like a lion they pin my hands and feet.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}I can count
all
my bones;
\par }{\Q my enemies are
gloating
over me in triumph.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}They are dividing
up my clothes
among themselves;
\par }{\Q they are rolling
dice
for
my garments.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}But you,
O
{\ND{Lord}}, do not
remain far away!
\par }{\Q You are my source of strength! Hurry
and help me!
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Deliver
me from the sword!
\par }{\Q Save my life
from the claws
of the wild dogs!
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Rescue
me from the mouth
of the lion,
\par }{\Q and from the horns
of the wild oxen!

\par }{\Q You have answered me!
\par }{\Q \VS{22}I will declare
your name
to my countrymen!

\par }{\Q In the middle
of the assembly
I will praise you!
\par }{\Q \VS{23}You loyal followers

\par }{\Q and rules

\par }{\Q Deliver

\par }{\Q \VS{17}O

\par }{\Q May they go wailing

\par }{\Q \VS{18}May lying

\par }{\Q lips

\par }{\Q with arrogance

\par }{\Q \VS{19}How

\par }{\Q which

\par }{\Q In plain sight of everyone you bestow

\par }{\Q \VS{20}You hide

\par }{\Q you conceal

\par }{\Q \VS{21}The
{\ND{Lord}}

\par }{\Q but he pays back

\par }{\Q all

\par }\PsalmChap{32}{\D 
By David;
a well-written song.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}How blessed

\par }{\Q whose sin is pardoned!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}How blessed

\par }{\Q I no

\par }{\Q \VS{8}I will instruct

\par }{\Q unless they are controlled
by
a bridle
and bit.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}An evil
person suffers
much pain,
\par }{\Q but
the
{\ND{Lord}}’s
faithfulness
overwhelms

\par }{\Q \VS{11}Rejoice
in the
{\ND{Lord}}
and be happy,
you who are godly!
\par }{\Q Shout
for joy, all
you who are morally
upright!


\par }\PsalmChap{33}{\PP \par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}You godly

\par }{\Q \VS{4}For

{\ND{Lord}}’s

\par }{\Q and everything

\par }{\Q \VS{5}The

\par }{\Q the

\par }{\Q Let all

\par }{\Q \VS{9}For

\par }{\Q \VS{10}The

\par }{\Q \VS{11}The

\par }{\Q his plans

{\ND{Lord}},
\par }{\Q the people

\par }{\Q \VS{13}The
{\ND{Lord}}

\par }{\Q he sees

\par }{\Q \VS{14}From the place

\par }{\Q at all

\par }{\Q \VS{15}He is the one who forms

\par }{\Q and takes note

\par }{\Q \VS{16}No

\par }{\Q a warrior

\par }{\Q despite its great

\par }{\Q \VS{18}Look,

\par }{\Q those who wait

\par }{\Q \VS{19}by saving

\par }{\Q and sustaining

\par }{\Q he is

\par }{\Q for

\par }{\Q \VS{22}May

{\ND{Lord}},

\par }{\Q for we wait for you.

\par }\PsalmChap{35}{\D 
By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O
{\ND{Lord}}, fight
those who fight
with me!
\par }{\Q Attack
those who attack me!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Grab
your small shield
and large shield,
\par }{\Q and rise
up to help me!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Use

and lance
against

me!
\par }{\Q Assure

your deliverer!”
\par }{\Q \VS{4}May those who seek
my life
be embarrassed
and humiliated!
\par }{\Q May those who
plan
to harm

\par }{\Q \VS{5}May they be
like wind-driven
chaff,
\par }{\Q as the
{\ND{Lord}}’s
angel
attacks them!
\par }{\Q \VS{6}May

be dark
and slippery,
\par }{\Q as the
{\ND{Lord}}’s
angel

\par }{\Q \VS{7}I did not harm
them, but they hid
a net
to catch me
\par }{\Q and dug

to trap me.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Let destruction
take

\par }{\Q Let the net
they hid
catch
them!
\par }{\Q Let them fall
into destruction!
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Then I
will rejoice
in the
{\ND{Lord}}
\par }{\Q and be happy

\par }{\Q \VS{10}With all

I will say,
\par }{\Q “O
{\ND{Lord}}, who

\par }{\Q You rescue
the oppressed
from

\par }{\Q the oppressed
and needy
from those who try to rob them.”
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Violent

\par }{\Q and falsely
accuse me.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}They repay
me evil
for
the good
I have done;

\par }{\Q I am overwhelmed
with sorrow.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}When they were sick,
I
wore
sackcloth,
\par }{\Q and refrained from eating food.
\par }{\Q (If I
am lying, may my prayers
go unanswered!)
\par }{\Q \VS{14}I mourned for them as I would for a friend
or my brother.
\par }{\Q I bowed down
in sorrow
as if I were mourning
for my mother.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}But when I stumbled,
they rejoiced
and gathered together;
\par }{\Q they gathered together
to ambush me.

\par }{\Q They tore
at me without
stopping to rest.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}When I tripped, they taunted
me relentlessly,

\par }{\Q and tried to bite me.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}O Lord,
how long
are you going to just stand there and watch
this?

\par }{\Q Rescue
me
from their destructive attacks;
\par }{\Q guard my life
from the young lions!
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Then I will give you thanks
in the great
assembly;
\par }{\Q I will praise
you before a large crowd
of people!
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Do not
let those who are my enemies
for no reason
gloat
over me!
\par }{\Q Do not let those who hate
me without cause
carry out their wicked schemes!
\par }{\Q \VS{20}For
they do not
try to make

with others,

\par }{\Q but plan
ways
to deceive
those who are unsuspecting.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}They are ready
to devour
me;

\par }{\Q they say,
“Aha! Aha! We’ve got you!”
\par }{\Q \VS{22}But you take notice,

{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q O Lord,
do not
remain far
away from me!
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Rouse

me!

\par }{\Q My God
and Lord,

\par }{\Q \VS{24}Vindicate

O
{\ND{Lord}}
my God!
\par }{\Q Do not
let them gloat over me!
\par }{\Q \VS{25}Do not
let them say
to themselves, “Aha! We have what we wanted!”

\par }{\Q Do not
let them say,
“We have devoured him!”
\par }{\Q \VS{26}May those who want to harm
me be totally
embarrassed
and ashamed!

\par }{\Q May those who arrogantly
taunt
me be covered with shame
and humiliation!
\par }{\Q \VS{27}May those who desire
my vindication

and rejoice!
\par }{\Q May they continually

{\ND{Lord}}
be praised,
for he wants
his servant
to be secure.”
\par }{\Q \VS{28}Then
I will tell others

\par }{\Q and praise

\par }\PsalmChap{36}{\D

\par }{\Q \VS{2}for

\par }{\Q to recognize

\par }{\Q he does not

\par }\PsalmChap{37}{\D 
By David.

\par }{\Q they will go up in smoke.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Evil

\par }{\Q but the godly

\par }{\Q \VS{24}Even if

\par }\PsalmChap{38}{\D 
A psalm
of David,
written
to get God’s attention.

\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O

{\ND{Lord}}, do not
continue
to rebuke
me in your anger!
\par }{\Q Do not continue to punish me in your raging fury!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}For
your arrows
pierce
me,
\par }{\Q and your hand
presses me down.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}My whole
body
is sick
because of your judgment;

\par }{\Q I
am deprived
of health
because
of my sin.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For
my sins
overwhelm
me;

\par }{\Q like a heavy
load,
they are too much for me to bear.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}My wounds
are infected
and starting
to smell,

\par }{\Q because
of my foolish sins.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I am dazed
and completely humiliated;
\par }{\Q all
day
long I walk
around mourning.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}For
I am overcome
with shame
\par }{\Q and my whole body
is sick.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}I am numb with pain
and severely
battered;
\par }{\Q I groan loudly
because of the anxiety
I feel.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}O Lord,
you understand my heart’s
desire;
\par }{\Q my groaning
is not
hidden
from you.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}My heart
beats quickly;
\par }{\Q my strength
leaves
me;
\par }{\Q I can hardly
see.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Because of my condition,
even my friends
and acquaintances
keep their distance;
\par }{\Q my neighbors stand
far away.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Those who seek
my life
try to entrap
me;

\par }{\Q those who want
to harm
me speak
destructive
words;
\par }{\Q all
day
long they say deceitful things.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}But I am
like a deaf man – I hear nothing;
\par }{\Q I am like a mute who cannot speak.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}I am like
a man
who
cannot
hear
\par }{\Q and is incapable
of arguing
his defense.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Yet
I wait
for
you, O
{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q You
will respond,
O Lord,
my God!
\par }{\Q \VS{16}I have prayed
for deliverance, because
otherwise
they will gloat
over me;

\par }{\Q when my foot
slips
they will arrogantly taunt me.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}For
I
am about
to stumble,
\par }{\Q and I am in
constant
pain.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Yes,
I confess
my wrongdoing,
\par }{\Q and I am concerned
about my sins.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}But those who are my enemies
for no reason are numerous;
\par }{\Q those who hate
me without cause outnumber me.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}They repay
me evil
for the good I have done;
\par }{\Q though I have tried to do good
to them,
they hurl accusations
at me.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Do not
abandon
me, O
{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q My God,
do not
remain far
away from me!
\par }{\Q \VS{22}Hurry
and help
me, O Lord,
my deliverer!


\par }\PsalmChap{39}{\D 
For the music director,
Jeduthun;
a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}I decided, “I will watch what I say
\par }{\Q and make sure
I do not
sin
with my
tongue.
\par }{\Q I will put a muzzle
over
my mouth
\par }{\Q while
in
the
presence of
an evil man.”
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I was stone
silent;
\par }{\Q I held back
the urge to speak.

\par }{\Q My frustration grew;
\par }{\Q \VS{3}my anxiety
intensified.
\par }{\Q As I thought about
it, I became impatient.
\par }{\Q Finally I spoke
these words:
\par }{\Q \VS{4}“O

{\ND{Lord}}, help me understand
my mortality
\par }{\Q and the brevity
of life!

\par }{\Q Let me realize
how quickly my life will pass!
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Look,
you make
my days
short-lived,
\par }{\Q and my life span
is nothing
from your perspective.
\par }{\Q Surely
all
people,
even those who
seem secure, are nothing but vapor.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Surely
people
go
through life as mere ghosts.
\par }{\Q Surely they accumulate
worthless
wealth
\par }{\Q without
knowing
who
will eventually haul it away.”
\par }{\Q \VS{7}But now,
O Lord,
upon what
am I relying?
\par }{\Q You are my only hope!
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Deliver
me from all
my sins of rebellion!
\par }{\Q Do not
make
me the object of
fools’
insults!
\par }{\Q \VS{9}I am silent
and cannot
open
my mouth
\par }{\Q because
of what you
have done.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Please stop
wounding

\par }{\Q You have almost beaten

all

\par }{\Q before

\par }{\Q our ancestors

\par }{\Q what

\par }{\Q in ancient

\par }{\Q and they did not

\par }{\Q and I do not

\par }{\Q you humiliate

\par }{\Q \VS{8}In God

\par }{\Q and we will continually

\par }{\Q \VS{9}But you rejected

\par }{\Q You did not

\par }{\Q Those who hate

\par }{\Q \VS{11}You handed

\par }{\Q you scattered

\par }{\Q \VS{12}You sold

for a pittance;
\par }{\Q you did not

\par }{\Q \VS{13}You made

\par }{\Q those who live on our borders

\par }{\Q \VS{14}You made

\par }{\Q foreigners

\par }{\Q \VS{15}All

\par }{\Q and am overwhelmed

\par }{\Q \VS{16}before

enemy
\par }{\Q who ridicules

has happened

\par }{\Q or

\par }{\Q \VS{18}We have not

\par }{\Q nor have we disobeyed

\par }{\Q \VS{19}Yet

\par }{\Q you have covered

\par }{\Q \VS{20}If

\par }{\Q and spread out

\par }{\Q \VS{21}would not

\par }{\Q for

\par }{\Q \VS{22}Yet because

all

\par }{\Q we are treated

at the slaughtering block.

O Lord?
\par }{\Q Wake

\par }{\Q \VS{24}Why

\par }{\Q and ignore

and mistreated?
\par }{\Q \VS{25}For
we lie in
the dirt,
\par }{\Q with
our bellies
pressed to the ground.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}Rise
up and help

\par }{\Q Rescue

of your loyal love!

is the destiny
of fools,

\par }{\Q and of those who approve of their philosophy.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{14}They will travel to Sheol
like sheep,
\par }{\Q with death
as their shepherd.
\par }{\Q The godly
will rule over
them when the day of vindication dawns;
\par }{\Q Sheol
will consume their bodies
and they will no longer live
in impressive houses.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}But
God
will rescue
my life
from the power
of Sheol;
\par }{\Q certainly
he will pull
me to safety. (Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Do not
be afraid
when
a man
becomes
rich
\par }{\Q and his wealth multiplies!
\par }{\Q \VS{17}For
he will take
nothing
with him when he dies;
\par }{\Q his wealth
will not
follow
him down
into the grave.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}He pronounces this
blessing
on himself
while he is alive:
\par }{\Q “May men praise
you, for
you have done well!”
\par }{\Q \VS{19}But he will join
his ancestors;
\par }{\Q they will never
again see
the light of day.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Wealthy
people
do not
understand;
\par }{\Q they are like
animals
that perish.


\par }\PsalmChap{50}{\D 
A psalm
by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}El,
God,
the {\ND{Lord}}
speaks,
\par }{\Q and summons
the earth
to come from the east
and west.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}From Zion,
the most
beautiful
of all places,

\par }{\Q God
comes in splendor.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Our God
approaches
and is not
silent;
\par }{\Q consuming
fire
goes ahead
of him
\par }{\Q and all around
him a storm rages.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}He summons
the heavens
above,
\par }{\Q as well as the earth,
so that he might judge
his people.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}He says:

\par }{\Q “Assemble
my covenant people
before me,

\par }{\Q those who ratified
a covenant
with me by
sacrifice!”
\par }{\Q \VS{6}The heavens
declare
his fairness,
\par }{\Q for
God
is judge.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{7}He says:

\par }{\Q “Listen
my people! I am speaking!
\par }{\Q Listen Israel! I am accusing
you!

\par }{\Q I am
God,
your God!
\par }{\Q \VS{8}I am not
condemning
you because of your sacrifices,
\par }{\Q or because of your burnt sacrifices
that you continually offer me.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}I do not
need to take
a bull
from your household
\par }{\Q or goats
from your sheepfolds.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}For
every
wild animal
in the forest
belongs to me,
\par }{\Q as well as the cattle
that graze on a thousand
hills.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}I
keep track
of every
bird
in the hills,
\par }{\Q and the insects
of the field
are mine.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Even if
I were hungry,
I would not
tell
you,
\par }{\Q for
the world
and all it contains belong to me.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Do I eat
the flesh
of bulls?
\par }{\Q Do I drink
the blood
of goats?
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Present
to God
a thank-offering!
\par }{\Q Repay
your vows
to the sovereign One!
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Pray
to me when
you are in trouble!

\par }{\Q I will deliver
you, and you will honor me!”
\par }{\Q \VS{16}God
says
this to the evildoer:

\par }{\Q “How
can you declare
my commands,
\par }{\Q and talk
about my covenant?
\par }{\Q \VS{17}For you
hate
instruction
\par }{\Q and reject
my words.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}When
you see
a thief,
you join
him;
\par }{\Q you associate
with
men
who are unfaithful
to their wives.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}You do damage
with words,
\par }{\Q and use
your tongue
to deceive.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}You plot against
your brother;
\par }{\Q you slander
your own brother.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}When you did
these
things, I was silent,
\par }{\Q so you thought
I was exactly like
you.

\par }{\Q But now
I will
condemn
you
\par }{\Q and state
my case against you!
\par }{\Q \VS{22}Carefully
consider
this,
you who reject
God!

\par }{\Q Otherwise
I will rip you to shreds
\par }{\Q and no
one will be able to rescue you.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Whoever presents a thank-offering
honors
me.

\par }{\Q To whoever obeys my commands,
I will reveal
my power
to deliver.”


\par }\PsalmChap{51}{\D 
For the music director;
a psalm
of David,
written when Nathan
the prophet
confronted
him after David’s affair
with
Bathsheba.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Have mercy
on me, O God,
because of your loyal love!
\par }{\Q Because of your great
compassion,
wipe away
my rebellious acts!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Wash
away my wrongdoing!

\par }{\Q Cleanse
me of my sin!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For
I
am aware
of my rebellious
acts;
\par }{\Q I am forever
conscious of my sin.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Against you – you above all – I have sinned;
\par }{\Q I have done what is evil in your sight.
\par }{\Q So you are just when you confront me;
\par }{\Q you are right when you condemn me.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Look,
I was guilty of sin
from birth,
\par }{\Q a sinner
the moment my mother
conceived me.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Look,
you desire
integrity in the inner man;
\par }{\Q you want me to possess
wisdom.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Sprinkle
me with water
and I will be pure;
\par }{\Q wash
me and I will be whiter
than snow.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Grant
me the ultimate joy
of being forgiven!

\par }{\Q May the bones
you crushed
rejoice!
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Hide
your face
from my sins!
\par }{\Q Wipe
away all
my guilt!
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Create
for me a pure
heart,
O God!

\par }{\Q Renew
a resolute
spirit
within me!
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Do not
reject
me!

\par }{\Q Do not
take
your Holy
Spirit
away from me!
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Let me again
experience the joy
of your deliverance!
\par }{\Q Sustain
me by giving me the desire to obey!
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Then I will teach
rebels
your merciful ways,
\par }{\Q and sinners
will turn
to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Rescue
me from the guilt of murder,
O God,
the God
who delivers
me!
\par }{\Q Then my tongue
will shout
for joy because of your deliverance.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}O Lord,
give me the words!

\par }{\Q Then
my mouth
will praise you.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Certainly
you do not
want
a sacrifice,
or else I would
offer it;

\par }{\Q you do not
desire a burnt sacrifice.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}The sacrifices
God
desires are a humble spirit –
\par }{\Q O God,
a humble and repentant
heart
you will
not
reject.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Because you favor
Zion,
do what
is good for her!

\par }{\Q Fortify
the walls
of Jerusalem!
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Then
you will accept
the proper
sacrifices,
burnt sacrifices
and whole
offerings;
\par }{\Q then
bulls
will be sacrificed
on
your altar.


\par }\PsalmChap{52}{\D 
For the music director;
a well-written song
by David.
It was written when Doeg
the Edomite
went
and informed
Saul: “David
has arrived
at
the home
of Ahimelech.”
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Why
do you boast
about your evil
plans, O powerful man?
\par }{\Q God’s
loyal love
protects me all
day long!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Your tongue
carries out your destructive
plans;
\par }{\Q it is as effective as a sharp
razor,
O deceiver.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}You love
evil
more than good,
\par }{\Q lies
more than speaking
the truth.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{4}You love
to use all
the words
that destroy,
\par }{\Q and the tongue
that deceives.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Yet
God
will make you a permanent heap of ruins.

\par }{\Q He will
scoop
you up and remove you from
your home;
\par }{\Q he will
uproot
you from
the land
of the living.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{6}When the godly
see
this, they will be
filled with awe,
\par }{\Q and will mock the evildoer, saying:
\par }{\Q \VS{7}“Look,
here is the man
who would not
make
God
his protector!
\par }{\Q He trusted
in his great
wealth
\par }{\Q and was confident
about his plans to destroy others.”
\par }{\Q \VS{8}But I am
like a flourishing
olive tree
in the house
of God;
\par }{\Q I continually
trust
in God’s
loyal love.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}I will continually
thank
you when
you execute
judgment;

\par }{\Q I will rely
on you,
for
your loyal followers
know
you are good.


\par }\PsalmChap{53}{\D 
For the music director;
{\IT{according to the
machalath}}
style; a well-written song
by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Fools
say
to themselves, “There is no
God.”
\par }{\Q They sin and commit
evil
deeds;

\par }{\Q none
of them does what
is right.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}God
looks
down from heaven
at the human
race,

\par }{\Q to see
if there is anyone
who is wise
and seeks
God.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Everyone
rejects
God;

\par }{\Q they are all
morally corrupt.
\par }{\Q None
of them does
what is right,
\par }{\Q not
even
one!
\par }{\Q \VS{4}All
those who behave
wickedly
do not
understand –
\par }{\Q those who devour
my people
as if they were eating
bread,
\par }{\Q and do not
call
out to God.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They are absolutely
terrified,
\par }{\Q even by things
that do not
normally
cause fear.
\par }{\Q For
God
annihilates
those
who attack you.

\par }{\Q You are able to humiliate
them because
God
has rejected them.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I wish
the deliverance
of Israel
would come from Zion!
\par }{\Q When God
restores the well-being
of his people,
\par }{\Q may
Jacob
rejoice,
\par }{\Q may Israel
be happy!


\par }\PsalmChap{54}{\D 
For the music director,
to be accompanied by stringed instruments;
a well-written song
by David.
It was written when the Ziphites
came
and informed
Saul: “David
is hiding
with
us.”

\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O God,
deliver
me by your name!

\par }{\Q Vindicate
me by your power!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}O God,
listen
to my prayer!
\par }{\Q Pay
attention
to what I say!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For
foreigners
attack me;

\par }{\Q ruthless
men, who do not
respect
God,
seek
my life.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Look,
God
is my deliverer!

\par }{\Q The Lord
is among those who
support
me.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}May
those who wait
to ambush me
be repaid
for their evil!

\par }{\Q As a demonstration
of your faithfulness,
destroy them!
\par }{\Q \VS{6}With a freewill
offering I will sacrifice
to you!
\par }{\Q I will give thanks
to your name,
O
{\ND{Lord}}, for
it is good!
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Surely
he rescues
me from
all
trouble,
\par }{\Q and I triumph
over my enemies.


\par }\PsalmChap{55}{\D 
For the music director,
to be accompanied by stringed instruments;
a well-written song
by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Listen,
O God,
to my prayer!
\par }{\Q Do not
ignore
my appeal for mercy!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Pay attention
to me and answer
me!
\par }{\Q I am so upset
and distressed,
I am beside myself,
\par }{\Q \VS{3}because of what
the enemy
says,

\par }{\Q and because of how the wicked
pressure
me,

\par }{\Q for
they hurl
trouble
down upon me

\par }{\Q and angrily
attack me.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}My heart
beats
violently within
me;
\par }{\Q the horrors
of death
overcome me.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Fear
and panic
overpower
me;

\par }{\Q terror
overwhelms me.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I say, “I wish
I had wings
like a dove!
\par }{\Q I would fly
away and settle in a safe place!
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Look,
I will escape
to a distant
place;
\par }{\Q I will stay
in the wilderness.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{8}I will hurry off
to a place
that is safe
\par }{\Q from the strong wind
and the gale.”
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Confuse
them, O Lord!
\par }{\Q Frustrate
their plans!

\par }{\Q For
I see
violence
and conflict
in the city.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Day
and night
they walk around
on
its walls,
\par }{\Q while wickedness
and destruction
are within it.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Disaster
is within
it;
\par }{\Q violence
and deceit
do not
depart
from its public square.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Indeed,
it is not
an enemy
who insults
me,
\par }{\Q or else I could bear
it;
\par }{\Q it is not
one who hates
me who arrogantly
taunts me,

\par }{\Q or else I could hide
from him.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}But it is you,
a man
like me,
\par }{\Q my close friend
in whom I confided.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}We would share personal
thoughts
with each other;

\par }{\Q in God’s
temple
we would walk
together
among the crowd.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}May death destroy
them!

\par }{\Q May they go down
alive
into Sheol!

\par }{\Q For
evil
is in their dwelling place
and in their midst.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}As for me, I
will call
out to
God,
\par }{\Q and the
{\ND{Lord}}
will deliver me.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}During the evening,
morning,
and noontime
\par }{\Q I will lament
and moan,
\par }{\Q and he will hear
me.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}He will rescue
me and protect
me from those who attack me,

\par }{\Q even though
they greatly outnumber
me.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}God,
the one who has
reigned
as king from long ago,
\par }{\Q will hear
and humiliate
them. (Selah)
\par }{\Q They refuse
to change,
\par }{\Q and do not
fear
God.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}He attacks
his friends;
\par }{\Q he breaks
his solemn promises to them.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}His words are as smooth
as butter,
\par }{\Q but he harbors animosity
in his heart.
\par }{\Q His words
seem softer
than oil,
\par }{\Q but they
are really like sharp swords.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}Throw
your burden
upon
the {\ND{Lord}},
\par }{\Q and he will sustain
you.

\par }{\Q He will never
allow
the godly
to be upended.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}But you,
O God,
will bring them down
to the deep Pit.
\par }{\Q Violent
and deceitful
people
will not
live even half a normal
lifespan.
\par }{\Q But as for me, I
trust in you.


\par }\PsalmChap{56}{\D 
For the music director;
{\IT{according to the
yonath-elem-rechovim}}
style; a prayer
of David,
written when the
Philistines
captured
him in Gath.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Have mercy
on me, O God,
for
men
are attacking
me!

\par }{\Q All
day
long hostile enemies
are tormenting me.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Those who anticipate
my defeat
attack me all
day
long.
\par }{\Q Indeed,
many
are fighting
against me, O Exalted One.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}When
I am
afraid,
\par }{\Q I
trust in you.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}In God
– I boast
in his promise –
\par }{\Q in God
I trust,
I am not
afraid.
\par }{\Q What
can mere
men do to me?
\par }{\Q \VS{5}All
day
long they cause me trouble;

\par }{\Q they make a habit
of plotting
my demise.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}They
stalk
and lurk;
\par }{\Q they
watch
my every step,

\par }{\Q as they prepare to take my life.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Because
they are bent on violence,
do not let them escape!

\par }{\Q In your anger
bring down
the nations,
O God!
\par }{\Q \VS{8}You keep
track
of my misery.
\par }{\Q Put
my tears
in your leather container!

\par }{\Q Are they not
recorded in your scroll?
\par }{\Q \VS{9}My enemies
will turn
back
when
I cry
out to you for help;

\par }{\Q I know
that
God is on my side.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}In God
– I boast
in his promise –
\par }{\Q in the
{\ND{Lord}}
–
I boast
in his promise –
\par }{\Q \VS{11}in God
I trust,
I am not
afraid.
\par }{\Q What
can mere men
do to me?
\par }{\Q \VS{12}I
am obligated
to fulfill
the vows
I made to you, O God;
\par }{\Q I will give you the thank-offerings you deserve,
\par }{\Q \VS{13}when
you deliver
my life
from death.
\par }{\Q You keep my feet
from stumbling,
\par }{\Q so that I might serve
God
as I enjoy life.


\par }\PsalmChap{57}{\D 
For the music director;
{\IT{according to the

a prayer

from Saul

on me, O God! Have mercy
on me!
\par }{\Q For

\par }{\Q In the shadow
of your wings
I take shelter
\par }{\Q until
trouble passes.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I cry
out for help to the sovereign
God,
\par }{\Q to the God
who vindicates me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}May he send
help from heaven
and deliver
me

\par }{\Q from my enemies
who hurl
insults! (Selah)
\par }{\Q May God
send
his loyal love
and faithfulness!
\par }{\Q \VS{4}I

\par }{\Q I lie down

\par }{\Q men

\par }{\Q whose tongues

sword.

the sky,
O God!
\par }{\Q May your splendor
cover the whole

\par }{\Q \VS{6}They have prepared
a net
to trap

\par }{\Q I am discouraged.
\par }{\Q They have dug
a pit
for me.

\par }{\Q They will fall
into
it! (Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{7}I am determined,
O God! I am determined!
\par }{\Q I will sing and praise you!
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Awake,
my
soul!

\par }{\Q Awake,
O stringed instrument
and harp!
\par }{\Q I will wake
up at dawn!
\par }{\Q \VS{9}I will give you thanks
before the nations,
O Master!
\par }{\Q I will sing praises
to you before foreigners!
\par }{\Q \VS{10}For
your loyal love
extends
beyond
the sky,
\par }{\Q and your faithfulness
reaches
the clouds.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Rise
up above
the sky,
O God!
\par }{\Q May your splendor
cover the whole
earth!


\par }\PsalmChap{58}{\D 
For the music director;
{\IT{according to the
al-tashcheth}} style;
a prayer
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Do you rulers really
pronounce
just
decisions?

\par }{\Q Do you judge
people
fairly?
\par }{\Q \VS{2}No! You plan
how to do what
is unjust;
\par }{\Q you deal
out violence
in the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}The wicked
turn aside
from birth;
\par }{\Q liars
go astray
as soon as they are born.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Their venom
is like
that of a snake,
\par }{\Q like
a deaf
serpent
that does not
hear,
\par }{\Q \VS{5}that
does not
respond
to the magicians,
\par }{\Q or to a
skilled snake-charmer.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}O God,

the teeth
in their mouths!
\par }{\Q Smash
the jawbones
of the lions,
O
{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Let
them disappear
like
water
that flows
away!

\par }{\Q Let them wither like
grass!
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Let them be like
a snail
that melts away
as it moves
along!

\par }{\Q Let them be like stillborn
babies
that never
see
the sun!
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Before
the kindling
is even placed under your pots,
\par }{\Q he will sweep it away
along with both the raw
and cooked meat.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}The godly
will rejoice
when
they see
vengeance
carried
out;
\par }{\Q they will bathe
their feet
in the blood
of the wicked.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Then observers
will say,
\par }{\Q “Yes
indeed, the godly
are rewarded!

\par }{\Q Yes indeed,
there is
a God
who judges
in the earth!”


\par }\PsalmChap{59}{\D 
For the music director;
{\IT{according to the
al-tashcheth}} style;
a prayer
of David,
written when Saul
sent
men to surround
his house
and murder him.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Deliver
me from my enemies,
my God!
\par }{\Q Protect
me from those who attack me!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Deliver
me from evildoers!

\par }{\Q Rescue
me from violent
men!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For
look,
they wait to ambush
me;
\par }{\Q powerful men stalk
me,
\par }{\Q but not
because
I have rebelled
or
sinned,
O
{\ND{Lord}}.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Though I have done nothing wrong, they
are anxious
to attack.

\par }{\Q Spring
into action
and help
me! Take notice of me!
\par }{\Q \VS{5}You,
O
{\ND{Lord}}
God,
the invincible
warrior, the God
of Israel,
\par }{\Q rouse
yourself and punish
all
the nations!
\par }{\Q Have no
mercy
on any
treacherous
evildoers! (Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{6}They return
in the evening;
\par }{\Q they growl
like a dog
\par }{\Q and prowl around outside
the city.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Look,
they hurl insults
at me
\par }{\Q and openly threaten to kill me,
\par }{\Q for
they say,

\par }{\Q “Who
hears?”
\par }{\Q \VS{8}But you,
O
{\ND{Lord}}, laugh
in disgust at them;

\par }{\Q you taunt
all
the nations.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}You are my source
of strength! I will wait for
you!

\par }{\Q For
God
is my refuge.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}The God
who loves
me
will help me;
\par }{\Q God
will enable
me to triumph over my enemies.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Do not
strike
them dead suddenly,
\par }{\Q because then
my people
might
forget
the lesson.

\par }{\Q Use your power to make them homeless vagabonds
and then bring them down,
\par }{\Q O Lord
who shields us!
\par }{\Q \VS{12}They speak
sinful
words.
\par }{\Q So let them be trapped
by their own pride
\par }{\Q and by the curses
and lies
they speak!
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Angrily
wipe
them out! Wipe
them out so they vanish!
\par }{\Q Let them
know
that
God
rules
\par }{\Q in Jacob
and to the ends
of the earth! (Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{14}They return
in the evening;
\par }{\Q they growl
like a dog
\par }{\Q and prowl around outside
the city.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}They
wander
around looking for something to eat;
\par }{\Q they refuse to sleep
until they are full.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}As for me, I
will sing
about your strength;
\par }{\Q I will praise
your loyal love
in the morning.
\par }{\Q For
you are my refuge
\par }{\Q and my place of shelter
when
I face trouble.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}You are my source of strength! I will sing praises
to you!

\par }{\Q For
God
is my refuge,
the God
who loves me.


\par }\PsalmChap{60}{\D 
For the music director;
according
{\IT{to the
shushan-eduth}} style;
a prayer
of David
written to instruct
others. It was written when he fought
against
Aram Naharaim
and Aram-Zobah.
That was when Joab
turned back
and struck down
12,000
Edomites
in the
Valley
of Salt.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O God,
you have rejected
us.

\par }{\Q You suddenly turned on
us in your anger.
\par }{\Q Please restore us!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}You made the earth
quake;
you split
it open.

\par }{\Q Repair
its breaches,
for
it is ready to fall.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}You have made your people
experience
hard
times;

\par }{\Q you have made us drink
intoxicating
wine.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}You have given
your loyal followers
a rallying flag,
\par }{\Q so that they might seek safety
from the bow. (Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Deliver
by your power
and answer
me,

\par }{\Q so that
the ones you love
may be safe.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}God
has spoken
in his sanctuary:

\par }{\Q “I will triumph! I will parcel
out Shechem;
\par }{\Q the Valley
of Succoth
I will measure off.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Gilead
belongs to me,
\par }{\Q as does Manasseh!

\par }{\Q Ephraim
is my helmet,
\par }{\Q Judah
my royal scepter.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Moab
is my washbasin.
\par }{\Q I will make
Edom
serve
me.

\par }{\Q I will shout in triumph
over
Philistia.”
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Who
will lead me into
the fortified
city?
\par }{\Q Who
will bring me
to Edom?
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Have you not
rejected
us, O
God?
\par }{\Q O God,
you do not
go
into battle
with our armies.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Give
us help
against the enemy,
\par }{\Q for any help
men
might offer is futile.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}By God’s
power
we will conquer;
\par }{\Q he
will trample down
our enemies.


\par }\PsalmChap{61}{\D 
For the music director;
to be played on a stringed instrument;
written by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O God,
hear
my cry for help!
\par }{\Q Pay attention
to my prayer!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}From the most remote
place on earth
\par }{\Q I call
out to you in my despair.
\par }{\Q Lead
me up
to an inaccessible
rocky summit!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Indeed,
you are my shelter,
\par }{\Q a strong
tower
that protects
me from the enemy.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}I will be a permanent
guest
in your home;
\par }{\Q I will find shelter
in
the protection
of your wings.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{5}For
you,
O God,
hear
my vows;
\par }{\Q you grant

that belongs
to your loyal followers.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Give
the king
long life!
\par }{\Q Make
his lifetime
span
several
generations!
\par }{\Q \VS{7}May he reign forever
before
God!
\par }{\Q Decree that your loyal love
and faithfulness
should protect him.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Then
I will sing praises
to your name
continually,
\par }{\Q as I fulfill
my vows
day
after day.


\par }\PsalmChap{62}{\D 
For the music director,
Jeduthun;
a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}For God
alone
I patiently wait;
\par }{\Q he is the one who delivers
me.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}He alone
is my protector
and deliverer.
\par }{\Q He is my refuge;
I will not
be upended.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}How
long
will you threaten
a man?
\par }{\Q All
of you are murderers,
\par }{\Q as dangerous as a leaning
wall
or an unstable
fence.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}They spend all their time
planning how
to bring
him down.

\par }{\Q They love to use deceit;

\par }{\Q they pronounce blessings
with their
mouths,
\par }{\Q but inwardly
they utter curses.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Patiently wait
for God
alone, my soul!

\par }{\Q For
he is the one who gives me confidence.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}He alone
is my protector
and deliverer.
\par }{\Q He is my refuge;
I will not
be upended.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}God
delivers
me and exalts
me;
\par }{\Q God
is my
strong
protector
and my shelter.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Trust
in him at all

you people!
\par }{\Q Pour
out your hearts
before

\par }{\Q God
is our shelter! (Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Men
are nothing but
a mere breath;
\par }{\Q human
beings are unreliable.
\par }{\Q When they are weighed in the scales,
\par }{\Q all of them together
are lighter than air.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Do not
trust
in what you can gain by oppression!

\par }{\Q Do not
put false confidence in what you can gain by robbery!

\par }{\Q If wealth
increases,
do not
become attached to it!
\par }{\Q \VS{11}God
has declared
one
principle;
\par }{\Q two
principles I have heard:

\par }{\Q God
is strong,
\par }{\Q \VS{12}and you, O Lord,
demonstrate loyal love.
\par }{\Q For
you
repay
men
for what they do.


\par }\PsalmChap{63}{\D 
A psalm
of David,
written when
he was in the Judean
wilderness.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O God,
you
are my God! I long
for you!

\par }{\Q My soul
thirsts
for you,
\par }{\Q my flesh
yearns
for you,
\par }{\Q in a dry
and parched
land
where there is no
water.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Yes,
in the sanctuary
I have
seen
you,

\par }{\Q and witnessed
your power
and splendor.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Because
experiencing
your loyal love
is better than
life
itself,
\par }{\Q my lips
will praise you.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For this reason
I will praise
you while I live;
\par }{\Q in your name
I will lift
up my hands.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}As
if with choice meat
you satisfy
my soul.
\par }{\Q My mouth
joyfully
praises you,
\par }{\Q \VS{6}whenever
I remember
you on
my bed,
\par }{\Q and think about
you during the nighttime
hours.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}For
you are
my deliverer;
\par }{\Q under your wings
I rejoice.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}My soul
pursues
you;

\par }{\Q your right hand
upholds me.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Enemies seek
to destroy
my life,
\par }{\Q but they
will descend
into the depths
of the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Each
one will be handed
over to the sword;
\par }{\Q their corpses
will be eaten by jackals.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}But the king
will rejoice
in God;
\par }{\Q everyone
who takes oaths
in his name will boast,
\par }{\Q for
the mouths
of those who speak
lies will be shut up.


\par }\PsalmChap{64}{\D 
For the music director;
a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Listen
to me, O God,
as I offer
my lament!
\par }{\Q Protect
my life
from the enemy’s
terrifying attacks.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Hide
me from the plots
of evil
men,
\par }{\Q from the crowd
of evildoers.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}They sharpen
their tongues
like a sword;
\par }{\Q they aim
their arrow,
a slanderous charge,
\par }{\Q \VS{4}in order to shoot
down the innocent in secluded places.
\par }{\Q They shoot
at him
suddenly
and are unafraid of retaliation.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They encourage
one another to carry
out their evil
deed.
\par }{\Q They plan how to hide
snares,
\par }{\Q and boast, “Who
will see them?”
\par }{\Q \VS{6}They devise
unjust
schemes;
\par }{\Q they disguise
a well-conceived plot.
\par }{\Q Man’s
inner
thoughts cannot be discovered.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}But God
will shoot
at them;
\par }{\Q suddenly
they will be
wounded
by an arrow.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Their
slander
will bring about their demise.
\par }{\Q All
who see

\par }{\Q \VS{9}and all

will fear.

has done,
\par }{\Q and reflect

\par }{\Q \VS{10}The godly

in the
{\ND{Lord}}
\par }{\Q and take shelter
in him.
\par }{\Q All
the morally
upright
will boast.


\par }\PsalmChap{65}{\D 
For the music director;
a psalm
of David,
a song.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Praise
awaits
you, O God,
in Zion.
\par }{\Q Vows
made to you are fulfilled.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}You hear
prayers;
\par }{\Q all
people approach
you.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Our record
of sins
overwhelms
me,
\par }{\Q but you
forgive
our acts of rebellion.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}How blessed
is the one whom you choose,
\par }{\Q and allow
to live
in your palace courts.
\par }{\Q May we be satisfied
with the good things
of your house
–
\par }{\Q your holy
palace.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}You answer
our prayers by performing
awesome
acts of deliverance,
\par }{\Q O God,
our savior.

\par }{\Q All
the ends
of the earth
trust
in you,

\par }{\Q as well
as those
living across
the wide
seas.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}You created
the mountains
by your power,
\par }{\Q and demonstrated
your strength.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}You calm
the raging
seas
\par }{\Q and their roaring
waves,
\par }{\Q as well as the commotion
made by the nations.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Even those living
in the most remote areas
are awestruck
by your acts;
\par }{\Q you cause those living
in the east
and west
to praise you.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}You visit
the earth
and give it rain;
\par }{\Q you make it rich
and fertile
\par }{\Q with overflowing streams
full
of water.
\par }{\Q You provide
grain
for them,

\par }{\Q for
you prepare the earth to yield its crops.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}You saturate
its furrows,
\par }{\Q and soak
its plowed ground.
\par }{\Q With rain showers
you soften its soil,
\par }{\Q and make its crops
grow.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}You crown
the year
with your good
blessings,

\par }{\Q and you leave
abundance
in your wake.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}The pastures
in the wilderness
glisten
with moisture,

\par }{\Q and the hills
are clothed
with joy.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}The meadows
are clothed
with sheep,
\par }{\Q and the valleys
are covered
with grain.
\par }{\Q They shout
joyfully, yes,
they sing.


\par }\PsalmChap{66}{\D

\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Shout

\par }{\Q \VS{2}Sing praises

\par }{\Q \VS{3}Say

\par }{\Q “How
awesome

\par }{\Q Because of your great

your enemies

\par }{\Q and sings praises

\par }{\Q His acts
on

\par }{\Q \VS{6}He turned

\par }{\Q they passed

\par }{\Q \VS{7}He rules

\par }{\Q he watches
the nations.
\par }{\Q Stubborn

\par }{\Q Loudly

\par }{\Q \VS{9}He preserves

\par }{\Q and does not

\par }{\Q \VS{10}For

tested
us;
\par }{\Q you purified

silver.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}You led

\par }{\Q you caused

\par }{\Q \VS{12}You allowed men

\par }{\Q we passed through

and water,
\par }{\Q but you brought

\par }{\Q and my mouth

cattle
and goats.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Come! Listen,
all

\par }{\Q I will declare
what

for me.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}I cried out
to

\par }{\Q and praised

\par }{\Q \VS{18}If

in my heart,
\par }{\Q the Lord
would not
have listened.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}However,
God

\par }{\Q he listened
to my prayer.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}God
deserves
praise,

\par }{\Q for he did not
reject
my prayer
\par }{\Q or abandon his love
for me!

\par }\PsalmChap{68}{\D 
For the music director;
by David,

a song.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}God

\par }{\Q his adversaries

from him.

before

\par }{\Q so the wicked
are destroyed
before
God.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}But the godly
are happy;
\par }{\Q they rejoice
before
God
\par }{\Q and are overcome

{\ND{Lord}}
is his name!

\par }{\Q and an advocate

\par }{\Q he frees

\par }{\Q before

\par }{\Q and with glittering

\par }{\Q \VS{17}God

\par }{\Q they number in the thousands.
\par }{\Q The Lord

\par }{\Q \VS{18}You ascend

\par }{\Q you have taken many

\par }{\Q You receive

\par }{\Q including even

\par }{\Q Indeed the
{\ND{Lord}}

\par }{\Q \VS{19}The Lord

\par }{\Q Day

\par }{\Q the God

\par }{\Q \VS{20}Our God

\par }{\Q the

\par }{\Q \VS{21}Indeed

of his enemies,
\par }{\Q the hairy

\par }{\Q \VS{22}The Lord

\par }{\Q I will bring

\par }{\Q \VS{23}so

\par }{\Q and your dogs

\par }{\Q \VS{24}They see

\par }{\Q the processions

\par }{\Q musicians

\par }{\Q and the princes

\par }{\Q along with the princes

\par }{\Q \VS{28}God

\par }{\Q \VS{29}as you come out of your temple

\par }{\Q Kings

\par }{\Q and the nations

\par }{\Q They humble themselves

\par }{\Q God scatters

\par }{\Q Ethiopia

\par }{\Q Sing praises

\par }{\Q \VS{33}to the one who rides

\par }{\Q Look! He thunders loudly.
\par }{\Q \VS{34}Acknowledge
God’s

\par }{\Q his sovereignty

\par }{\Q and the power

\par }{\Q \VS{35}You are awe-inspiring,
O God,

\par }{\Q It is
the God

who gives

and strength.
\par }{\Q God

\par }\PsalmChap{69}{\D 
For the music director;
according to
the tune of “Lilies;”
by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Deliver
me, O God,
\par }{\Q for
the water
has reached
my neck.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I sink
into the deep
mire
\par }{\Q where there is no
solid ground;
\par }{\Q I am in
deep
water,
\par }{\Q and the current
overpowers me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}I am
exhausted
from shouting for help;
\par }{\Q my throat
is sore;
\par }{\Q my eyes
grow tired of looking
for my God.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Those who hate
me without cause
are more numerous
than the hairs
of my head.
\par }{\Q Those who want
to destroy
me, my enemies
for no reason,
outnumber me.

\par }{\Q They make me repay
what
I did not
steal!
\par }{\Q \VS{5}O God,
you
are aware
of my foolish
sins;

\par }{\Q my guilt
is not
hidden from you.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Let
none who rely
on you be disgraced
because of me,
\par }{\Q O sovereign

{\ND{Lord}}
and king!

\par }{\Q Let
none
who seek
you be ashamed
because of me,
\par }{\Q O God
of Israel!
\par }{\Q \VS{7}For
I suffer
humiliation
for your sake

\par }{\Q and am thoroughly
disgraced.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}My own brothers
treat
me like a stranger;
\par }{\Q they act as if I were a foreigner.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Certainly
zeal
for your house
consumes
me;
\par }{\Q I endure the insults
of those who insult you.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}I weep
and refrain from eating food,
\par }{\Q which causes

\par }{\Q and they

\par }{\Q O God,
