\par }\PsalmChap{73}{\D 
A psalm
by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Certainly
God
is good
to Israel,
\par }{\Q and to those whose motives
are pure!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}But as for me,
my feet
almost
slipped;
\par }{\Q my feet
almost
slid out from under me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For
I envied
those who are proud,
\par }{\Q as I observed
the prosperity
of the wicked.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For
they suffer
no
pain;
\par }{\Q their bodies
are strong
and well-fed.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They are immune
to the trouble
common to
men;
\par }{\Q they do not
suffer
as other men do.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Arrogance
is their necklace,
\par }{\Q and violence
their clothing.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Their prosperity
causes
them to do
wrong;

\par }{\Q their thoughts
are sinful.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}They mock
and say
evil things;
\par }{\Q they proudly
threaten
violence.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}They speak
as if they rule in heaven,
\par }{\Q and lay claim
to the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Therefore
they
have more than enough
food to eat,
\par }{\Q and even suck up
the water of the sea.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}They say,
“How
does God
know
what we do?
\par }{\Q Is
the sovereign one
aware of what goes on?”
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Take a good look! This
is what the wicked
are like,

\par }{\Q those who always
have it so easy
and get richer
and richer.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}I concluded, “Surely
in vain
I have kept my motives
pure
\par }{\Q and maintained
a pure
lifestyle.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}I suffer
all
day
long,
\par }{\Q and am punished
every morning.”
\par }{\Q \VS{15}If
I had publicized
these thoughts,

\par }{\Q I would have betrayed
your loyal followers.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}When I tried
to make sense
of this,
\par }{\Q it
was troubling
to me.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Then I entered
the precincts of God’s
temple,
\par }{\Q and understood
the destiny of the wicked.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Surely
you put
them in slippery places;
\par }{\Q you bring
them down
to ruin.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}How
desolate
they become
in a mere moment!
\par }{\Q Terrifying judgments
make their demise
complete!
\par }{\Q \VS{20}They are like a dream
after one wakes up.
\par }{\Q O Lord,
when you awake
you will despise
them.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Yes,
my spirit
was bitter,
\par }{\Q and my insides
felt sharp pain.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}I
was ignorant
and lacked insight;
\par }{\Q I was as senseless
as an animal before you.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}But I
am continually
with
you;
\par }{\Q you hold
my right
hand.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}You guide me by your wise advice,
\par }{\Q and then
you will lead
me to a position
of honor.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}Whom
do I have in heaven
but you?
\par }{\Q I desire
no
one but you on earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}My flesh
and my heart
may grow
weak,

\par }{\Q but God
always
protects
my heart
and gives me stability.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}Yes,
look! Those far from you
die;
\par }{\Q you destroy
everyone
who is unfaithful to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}But as for me, God’s
presence
is
all
I
need.

\par }{\Q I have made the sovereign

{\ND{Lord}}
my shelter,
\par }{\Q as I declare
all
the things you have done.

by Asaph.

\par }{\Q Has his promise
failed
forever?
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Has God
forgotten
to be merciful?
\par }{\Q Has his anger
stifled
his compassion?”
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Then I said,
“I am sickened
by the thought
\par }{\Q that the sovereign
One might become inactive.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}I will remember
the works
of the
{\ND{Lord}}.
\par }{\Q Yes,
I will remember
the amazing
things you did long ago!
\par }{\Q \VS{12}I will think
about all
you have done;
\par }{\Q I will reflect upon
your deeds!”
\VS{13}\par }{\Q O God,
your deeds
are extraordinary!

\par }{\Q What
god
can compare
to our great
God?
\par }{\Q \VS{14}You
are the God
who does
amazing
things;
\par }{\Q you have revealed
your strength
among the nations.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}You delivered
your people
by your strength –
\par }{\Q the children
of Jacob
and Joseph.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{16}The waters
saw
you, O God,
\par }{\Q the waters
saw
you and trembled.
\par }{\Q Yes,
the depths
of the sea shook with fear.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}The clouds
poured down
rain;
\par }{\Q the skies
thundered.
\par }{\Q Yes,
your arrows
flashed about.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Your thunderous
voice
was heard in the wind;
\par }{\Q the lightning bolts
lit
up the world;
\par }{\Q the earth
trembled
and shook.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}You walked through
the sea;
\par }{\Q you passed through
the surging
waters,
\par }{\Q but left no
footprints.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}You led
your people
like a flock
of sheep,
\par }{\Q by the hand
of Moses
and Aaron.


\par }\PsalmChap{78}{\D 
A well-written song
by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Pay attention,
my people,
to my instruction!
\par }{\Q Listen

I speak!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I will sing

\par }{\Q I will make

\par }{\Q \VS{3}What

\par }{\Q that which our ancestors

\par }{\Q \VS{4}we will not

\par }{\Q We will tell

{\ND{Lord}}’s

\par }{\Q he set up

\par }{\Q to make his deeds known

\par }{\Q and they will obey his commands.

\par }{\Q who were a stubborn

\par }{\Q a generation

\par }{\Q and faithful

\par }{\Q but they retreated

\par }{\Q and made the water

\par }{\Q \VS{17}Yet

\par }{\Q and rebelled

\par }{\Q by asking

\par }{\Q \VS{19}They insulted

\par }{\Q streams

\par }{\Q Will he provide

\par }{\Q \VS{21}When the
{\ND{Lord}}

\par }{\Q and did not

\par }{\Q and opened

\par }{\Q he gave

\par }{\Q he gave

\par }{\Q their food

\par }{\Q and filled with terror.

\par }{\Q and turned

\par }{\Q to the birds
of the sky;
\par }{\Q the flesh

\par }{\Q to the beasts
of the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}They have made

\par }{\Q all around

\par }{\Q \VS{4}We have become

\par }{\Q those who live on our borders

\par }{\Q \VS{5}How

{\ND{Lord}}?

\par }{\Q How long will your rage

\par }{\Q on

\par }{\Q and destroyed

\par }{\Q \VS{8}Do not

\par }{\Q Quickly

\par }{\Q for

\par }{\Q be avenged

\par }{\Q \VS{13}Then we,
your people,
the sheep
of your pasture,
\par }{\Q will continually
thank
you.

\par }{\Q We will tell
coming generations
of your praiseworthy acts.

\par }\PsalmChap{83}{\D

\par }{\Q those who hate

\par }{\Q \VS{18}Then they will know
that

{\ND{Lord}},

\par }{\Q the sovereign

\par }\PsalmChap{84}{\D

\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}How
lovely

\par }{\Q O
{\ND{Lord}}

\par }{\Q \VS{2}I desperately

\par }{\Q in the courts

{\ND{Lord}}’s

\par }{\Q My heart
and my entire

for joy
\par }{\Q to

\par }{\Q \VS{3}Even

\par }{\Q and the swallow

\par }{\Q where

\par }{\Q near your altars,

{\ND{Lord}}

\par }{\Q and praise

\par }{\Q he provides

\par }{\Q Listen,

\par }{\Q \VS{9}O God,

\par }{\Q than spending

\par }\PsalmChap{88}{\D 
A song,
a psalm
written by the Korahites;
for the music director;
according to
{\IT{the
machalath-leannoth}} style;
a well-written song
by Heman
the Ezrachite.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O
{\ND{Lord}}
God
who delivers
me!

\par }{\Q By day
I cry out
\par }{\Q and at night
I pray before you.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Listen to my prayer!

\par }{\Q Pay attention
to my cry for help!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For
my life
is filled
with troubles
\par }{\Q and I am ready to enter
Sheol.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}They treat
me like
those who descend
into the grave.
\par }{\Q I am
like a helpless
man,
\par }{\Q \VS{5}adrift
among the dead,
\par }{\Q like

lying
in the grave,
\par }{\Q whom

no
more,
\par }{\Q and who are
cut off
from your power.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}You place me in
the lowest
regions
of the pit,
\par }{\Q in the dark places, in
the watery
depths.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Your anger
bears
down on me,
\par }{\Q and you overwhelm me with all
your waves.
(Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{8}You cause
those who know
me
to keep their distance;
\par }{\Q you make
me an appalling
sight to them.
\par }{\Q I am trapped
and cannot
get free.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}My eyes
grow weak
because of oppression.
\par }{\Q I call
out to you, O
{\ND{Lord}}, all
day
long;
\par }{\Q I spread
out my hands in prayer to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Do
you accomplish
amazing things
for the dead?
\par }{\Q Do
the departed spirits
rise up
and give you thanks? (Selah)
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Is your loyal love
proclaimed
in the grave,
\par }{\Q or your faithfulness
in the place of the dead?
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Are your amazing
deeds experienced
in the dark
region,

\par }{\Q or your deliverance
in the land
of oblivion?
\par }{\Q \VS{13}As
for me,
I
cry out
to you, O
{\ND{Lord}};
\par }{\Q in the morning
my prayer
confronts you.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}O

{\ND{Lord}}, why
do you reject
me,
\par }{\Q and pay no attention to me?
\par }{\Q \VS{15}I am
oppressed
and have been on
the verge
of death since
my youth.
\par }{\Q I have been
subjected
to your horrors
and am numb
with pain.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Your anger
overwhelms
me;

\par }{\Q your terrors
destroy me.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}They surround
me like water
all
day
long;
\par }{\Q they join forces and encircle me.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}You cause
my friends
and neighbors
to keep their distance;

\par }{\Q those who know
me leave me alone in the darkness.

\par }\PsalmChap{90}{\D 
A prayer
of Moses,
the man
of God.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O Lord,
you
have been our protector
through all generations!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Even before
the mountains
came into existence,
\par }{\Q or you brought the world
into being,

\par }{\Q you were the eternal
God.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}You make mankind
return
to the dust,
\par }{\Q and say,
“Return,
O people!”
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Yes,
in your eyes
a thousand
years
\par }{\Q are like yesterday
that
quickly passes,
\par }{\Q or like one of the divisions of the nighttime.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}You bring their lives
to an end
and they “fall
asleep.”
\par }{\Q In the morning
they are like the grass
that sprouts up;
\par }{\Q \VS{6}in the morning
it glistens
and sprouts
up;
\par }{\Q at evening
time it withers
and dries up.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Yes,
we are consumed
by your anger;
\par }{\Q we are terrified
by your wrath.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}You are aware
of our sins;
\par }{\Q you even know about our hidden sins.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Yes,
throughout all
our days
we experience
your raging fury;
\par }{\Q the years
of our lives pass quickly,
like
a sigh.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}The days
of our lives
add up to seventy
years,
\par }{\Q or eighty,
if
one is especially strong.
\par }{\Q But even one’s best
years
are marred by trouble
and oppression.
\par }{\Q Yes,
they pass
quickly
and we fly away.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Who can
really fathom
the intensity
of your
anger?

\par }{\Q Your raging fury
causes people to fear you.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}So teach
us to consider
our mortality,
\par }{\Q so that
we might live
wisely.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Turn back
toward us, O
{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q How long
must this suffering
last?

\par }{\Q Have pity
on
your servants!
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Satisfy
us in the morning
with your loyal love!
\par }{\Q Then we will shout
for joy and be happy
all
our days!
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Make us happy
in proportion to the days
you have afflicted
us,
\par }{\Q in proportion to the years
we have experienced
trouble!
\par }{\Q \VS{16}May your servants
see your work!

\par }{\Q May their sons
see
your majesty!
\par }{\Q \VS{17}May
our sovereign
God
extend his favor
to
us!

\par }{\Q Make our endeavors
successful!

\par }{\Q Yes, make them successful!

\par }\PsalmChap{92}{\D

{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q Your plans are

\par }{\Q they are

\par }\PsalmChap{101}{\D 
A psalm

\par }{\Q \VS{2}I will walk in

\par }{\Q When
will you come

\par }{\Q I will conduct

\par }{\Q \VS{3}I will not

is dishonest.
\par }{\Q I hate
doing
evil;
\par }{\Q I will have no
part of it.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}I will have nothing
to do with a perverse
person;

\par }{\Q I
will not permit
evil.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}I will destroy
anyone who slanders
his neighbor
in secret.
\par }{\Q I will not
tolerate
anyone who has a cocky
demeanor
and an arrogant attitude.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I will favor
the honest
people of the land,
\par }{\Q and allow them to live
with me.
\par }{\Q Those who walk
in the way
of integrity
will attend me.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Deceitful
people will not
live
in

\par }{\Q Liars
will not
be welcome
in my presence.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Each morning

all
the wicked
people in the land,
\par }{\Q and remove
all
evildoers
from the city
of the {\ND{Lord}}.


\par }\PsalmChap{102}{\D 
The prayer
of an oppressed
man, as he grows faint
and pours out
his lament
before
the {\ND{Lord}}.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O
{\ND{Lord}}, hear
my prayer!
\par }{\Q Pay attention to my cry
for help!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Do not
ignore
me in my time
of trouble!

\par }{\Q Listen
to
me!

\par }{\Q When
I call
out to you, quickly
answer me!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For
my days
go up
in smoke,
\par }{\Q and my bones
are charred
like a fireplace.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}My heart
is parched
and withered
like grass,
\par }{\Q for
I am unable
to eat
food.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Because of the anxiety that makes me groan,
\par }{\Q my bones
protrude from my skin.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I
am like an owl
in the wilderness;
\par }{\Q I am like a screech owl
among the ruins.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}I stay awake;
\par }{\Q I am like
a solitary
bird
on
a roof.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}All
day
long my enemies
taunt
me;
\par }{\Q those who mock
me use my name in their curses.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}For
I eat
ashes
as if they were bread,
\par }{\Q and mix
my drink
with my tears,
\par }{\Q \VS{10}because
of your anger
and raging
fury.
\par }{\Q Indeed,
you pick
me up and throw me away.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}My days
are coming to an end,
\par }{\Q and I am
withered
like grass.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}But you,
O
{\ND{Lord}}, rule forever,
\par }{\Q and your reputation
endures.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}You
will rise
up and have compassion
on Zion.
\par }{\Q For
it is time
to have mercy
on her,
\par }{\Q for
the appointed
time has come.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Indeed,
your servants
take delight
in her stones,
\par }{\Q and feel compassion
for the dust of her ruins.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}The nations
will respect
the
reputation
of the {\ND{Lord}},

\par }{\Q and all
the kings
of the earth
will respect his splendor,
\par }{\Q \VS{16}when
the {\ND{Lord}}
rebuilds
Zion,
\par }{\Q and reveals
his splendor,
\par }{\Q \VS{17}when
he responds
to
the prayer
of the destitute,
\par }{\Q and does not
reject
their request.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}The account of his intervention will be recorded
for future generations;
\par }{\Q people
yet to be born
will praise
the
{\ND{Lord}}.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}For
he will look
down from his sanctuary
above;
\par }{\Q from heaven
the {\ND{Lord}}
will look
toward earth,
\par }{\Q \VS{20}in order to hear
the painful
cries of the prisoners,
\par }{\Q and to set free
those condemned to die,
\par }{\Q \VS{21}so they may proclaim
the name
of the {\ND{Lord}}
in Zion,
\par }{\Q and praise
him in Jerusalem,
\par }{\Q \VS{22}when the nations
gather
together,
\par }{\Q and the kingdoms
pay tribute
to the
{\ND{Lord}}.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}He has taken away
my strength
in the middle of life;

\par }{\Q he has cut short
my days.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}I say,
“O my God,
please do not
take me away in the middle
of my life!

\par }{\Q You endure through all generations.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}In earlier
times you established
the earth;
\par }{\Q the skies
are your handiwork.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}They
will perish,
\par }{\Q but you
will endure.
\par }{\Q They will wear out
like a garment;
\par }{\Q like clothes
you will remove
them and they will disappear.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}But you
remain;

\par }{\Q your years
do not come to an end.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}The children
of your servants
will settle
down here,
\par }{\Q and their descendants
will live securely
in your presence.”


\par }\PsalmChap{103}{\D 
By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Praise
the {\ND{Lord}}, O my soul!
\par }{\Q With all
that is within
me, praise his holy
name!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Praise
the {\ND{Lord}}, O my soul!
\par }{\Q Do not
forget
all
his kind deeds!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}He
is the one who forgives
all

\par }{\Q who heals
all

\par }{\Q \VS{4}who delivers
your life
from the Pit,
\par }{\Q who crowns

and compassion,
\par }{\Q \VS{5}who satisfies
your life with good

\par }{\Q so your youth
is renewed
like an eagle’s.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}The
{\ND{Lord}}
does
what is fair,
\par }{\Q and executes justice
for all
the oppressed.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}The
{\ND{Lord}} revealed
his faithful
acts to Moses,
\par }{\Q his deeds
to the Israelites.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}The
{\ND{Lord}}
is compassionate
and merciful;
\par }{\Q he is patient
and demonstrates great
loyal love.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}He does not
always
accuse,
\par }{\Q and does not
stay angry.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}He does not
deal with us as our sins
deserve;

\par }{\Q he does
not
repay us as our misdeeds deserve.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}For
as the skies
are high
above
the earth,
\par }{\Q so his loyal love
towers
over
his faithful followers.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}As far
as the eastern
horizon is from the west,
\par }{\Q so he removes
the guilt of our rebellious
actions from us.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}As a father
has compassion
on
his children,
\par }{\Q so the
{\ND{Lord}}
has compassion
on
his faithful followers.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}For
he knows
what we are made of;

\par }{\Q he realizes
we are made of clay.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}A person’s
life
is like grass.
\par }{\Q Like a flower
in the field
it flourishes,
\par }{\Q \VS{16}but when
the hot wind
blows by,
it disappears,
\par }{\Q and one can
no
longer
even spot
the place where it once grew.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}But the
{\ND{Lord}}
continually
shows loyal love
to his faithful followers,
\par }{\Q and is faithful
to their descendants,
\par }{\Q \VS{18}to those who keep
his covenant,
\par }{\Q who are careful
to obey
his commands.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}The
{\ND{Lord}}
has established
his throne
in heaven;
\par }{\Q his kingdom
extends
over everything.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Praise
the {\ND{Lord}}, you angels
of his,
\par }{\Q you powerful
warriors
who carry
out his decrees
\par }{\Q and obey
his orders!

\par }\PsalmChap{104}{\PP \par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Praise
the {\ND{Lord}}, O my soul!
\par }{\Q O
{\ND{Lord}}
my God,
you are magnificent.
\par }{\Q You are robed
in splendor
and majesty.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}He covers
himself with light
as if it were a garment.
\par }{\Q He stretches
out the skies
like a tent curtain,
\par }{\Q \VS{3}and lays the beams
of the upper rooms
of his palace on the rain clouds.
\par }{\Q He makes
the clouds
his chariot,
\par }{\Q and travels along
on
the wings
of the wind.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}He makes
the winds
his messengers,
\par }{\Q and the flaming
fire
his attendant.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}He established
the earth
on
its foundations;
\par }{\Q it will never be upended.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}The watery deep
covered

\par }{\Q the waters
reached above

\par }{\Q \VS{7}Your shout made the waters retreat;
\par }{\Q at

\par }{\Q \VS{8}as the mountains
rose up,
\par }{\Q and the valleys
went down
–
\par }{\Q to

for them.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}You set
up a boundary

cross,
\par }{\Q so that they would not
cover
the earth

\par }{\Q \VS{10}He turns
springs
into streams;
\par }{\Q they flow between
the mountains.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}They provide water
for all

in the field;
\par }{\Q the wild donkeys
quench

\par }{\Q \VS{12}The birds
of the sky

\par }{\Q they chirp

\par }{\Q \VS{13}He waters

\par }{\Q the earth

\par }{\Q \VS{14}He provides grass
for the cattle,
\par }{\Q and crops
for

to cultivate,
\par }{\Q so they can produce

from
the ground,
\par }{\Q \VS{15}as well as wine
that makes people
feel
so good,
\par }{\Q and so they can have oil
to make their faces

\par }{\Q as well as food
that sustains
people’s
lives.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}The trees
of the {\ND{Lord}}

\par }{\Q the cedars
of Lebanon
which
he planted,
\par }{\Q \VS{17}where
the birds
make nests,
\par }{\Q near the evergreens
in which the herons live.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}The wild goats
live in the high

\par }{\Q the rock badgers
find safety
in the cliffs.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}He made
the moon
to mark the months,
\par }{\Q and the sun
sets
according to a regular schedule.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}You make
it dark
and night
comes,
\par }{\Q during which
all
the beasts
of the forest
prowl around.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}The lions
roar
for prey,
\par }{\Q seeking
their food
from God.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}When the sun
rises,
they withdraw
\par }{\Q and sleep
in
their dens.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Men
then go out
to do their work,
\par }{\Q and labor
away until
evening.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}How
many

{\ND{Lord}}!

\par }{\Q You have exhibited
great skill
in making
all

\par }{\Q the earth
is full of the living things you have made.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}Over here
is the deep,
wide
sea,
\par }{\Q which
teems
with innumerable
swimming creatures,
\par }{\Q living things
both small
and large.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}The ships
travel
there,
\par }{\Q and over here swims the whale
you made
to play in it.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}All
of your creatures
wait for you
\par }{\Q to provide them
with food
on a regular basis.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}You give
food to them and they
receive

\par }{\Q you open

with food.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}When you ignore

\par }{\Q When you take away

\par }{\Q and return

\par }{\Q \VS{30}When you send
your life-giving breath,

\par }{\Q and you replenish
the surface
of the ground.
\par }{\Q \VS{31}May
the splendor
of the {\ND{Lord}}
endure!

\par }{\Q May the
{\ND{Lord}}
find pleasure
in the living things he has made!
\par }{\Q \VS{32}He looks
down on the earth
and it shakes;
\par }{\Q he touches
the mountains
and they start to smolder.
\par }{\Q \VS{33}I will sing
to the
{\ND{Lord}}
as long as I live;
\par }{\Q I will sing
praise to my God

\par }{\Q \VS{34}May my thoughts

\par }{\Q I

in the
{\ND{Lord}}.
\par }{\Q \VS{35}May sinners

\par }{\Q and the wicked

\par }{\Q Praise
the {\ND{Lord}}, O my soul!

{\ND{Lord}}!

{\ND{Lord}}’s

a psalm
of David.

O God!
\par }{\Q I will sing
and praise

and harp!
\par }{\Q I will wake

{\ND{Lord}}!
\par }{\Q I will sing praises

\par }{\Q \VS{4}For

extends
beyond the sky,
\par }{\Q and your faithfulness
reaches
the clouds.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Rise
up above

O God!
\par }{\Q May your splendor
cover the whole
earth!
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Deliver
by your power

\par }{\Q so that
the ones you love
may be safe.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}God
has spoken
in his sanctuary:

\par }{\Q “I will triumph! I will parcel
out Shechem,
\par }{\Q the valley
of Succoth
I will measure off.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Gilead
belongs to me,
\par }{\Q as does Manasseh!

\par }{\Q Ephraim
is my helmet,
\par }{\Q Judah
my royal scepter.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Moab
is my wash basin.
\par }{\Q I will make
Edom
serve
me.

\par }{\Q I will shout in triumph
over
Philistia.”
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Who
will lead me into
the fortified
city?
\par }{\Q Who
will bring me
to Edom?
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Have you not
rejected

\par }{\Q O God,

go
into battle with our armies.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Give

against the enemy,
\par }{\Q for any help
men
might offer is futile.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}By God’s

we will conquer;
\par }{\Q he
will trample down
our enemies.


\par }\PsalmChap{109}{\D 
For the music director,
a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O God
whom I praise,

ignore me!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}For

\par }{\Q they lie to me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}They surround

\par }{\Q they attack

\par }{\Q \VS{4}They repay

with accusations,
\par }{\Q but I

\par }{\Q \VS{5}They repay

for

\par }{\Q and hate
for

\VS{6}\par }{\Q Appoint
an evil
man to testify against him!

\par }{\Q May an accuser
stand

\par }{\Q \VS{7}When he is judged,

\par }{\Q Then his prayer
will be regarded as sinful.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}May

be few!

\par }{\Q May another

\par }{\Q \VS{9}May

\par }{\Q and his wife

\par }{\Q \VS{10}May

\par }{\Q asking

\par }{\Q May

\par }{\Q \VS{12}May no

\par }{\Q May no

\par }{\Q \VS{16}For

\par }{\Q he harassed
the oppressed
and needy,
\par }{\Q and killed
the disheartened.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}He loved
to curse others, so those
curses
have come
upon him.

\par }{\Q He had
no
desire
to bless anyone, so he has experienced
no blessings.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}He made

\par }{\Q so curses poured

\par }{\Q and seeped

\par }{\Q \VS{19}May

\par }{\Q \VS{20}May the

in this

\par }{\Q those who say

\par }{\Q \VS{21}O sovereign
{\SC{
Lord}},

\par }{\Q intervene

\par }{\Q Because

\par }{\Q \VS{22}For

\par }{\Q and my heart

\par }{\Q \VS{23}I am fading

\par }{\Q I am shaken

\par }{\Q I

\par }{\SH ב ({\IT{Bet}})
\par }{\Q \VS{9}How can a young person maintain a pure life?

\par }\PsalmChap{120}{\D 
A song
of ascents.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}In my distress
I cried
out
\par }{\Q to
the {\ND{Lord}}
and he answered me.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I said, “O
{\ND{Lord}},
rescue
me

\par }{\Q from those
who lie
with their lips
\par }{\Q and those who deceive
with their tongue.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}How
will
he severely
punish you,
\par }{\Q you deceptive
talker?
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Here’s how! With the sharp
arrows
of warriors,
\par }{\Q with
arrowheads
forged over the hot coals.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}How miserable
I am!

\par }{\Q For
I have lived temporarily
in Meshech;
\par }{\Q I have resided among
the tents
of Kedar.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}For too long
I have had to reside
\par }{\Q with
those who hate
peace.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}I
am committed to peace,
\par }{\Q but when I speak,
they
want to make war.


\par }\PsalmChap{121}{\D 
A song
of ascents.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}I look
up toward
the hills.
\par }{\Q From where
does my help
come?
\par }{\Q \VS{2}My help
comes
from the
{\ND{Lord}},

\par }{\Q the Creator
of heaven
and earth!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}May he not
allow
your foot
to slip!
\par }{\Q May your protector
not
sleep!
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Look! Israel’s
protector
\par }{\Q does not
sleep
or
slumber!
\par }{\Q \VS{5}The
{\ND{Lord}}
is your protector;
\par }{\Q the {\ND{Lord}}
is the shade
at your right hand.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}The sun
will not
harm
you by day,
\par }{\Q or the moon
by night.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}The
{\ND{Lord}}
will protect
you from all
harm;
\par }{\Q he will protect
your life.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}The
{\ND{Lord}}
will protect
you in all you do,
\par }{\Q now
and forevermore.


\par }\PsalmChap{122}{\D 
A song
of ascents,
by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}I was glad

\par }{\Q “We will go
to the
{\ND{Lord}}’s

\par }{\Q \VS{2}Our feet

\par }{\Q inside your gates,

\par }{\Q the tribes

\par }{\Q \VS{6}Pray
for the peace

\par }{\Q May those who love

\par }\PsalmChap{139}{\D 
For the music director,
a psalm
of David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}O
{\ND{Lord}}, you examine
me and know.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}You
know
when I sit
down and when I get
up;
\par }{\Q even from far
away you understand
my motives.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}You carefully observe
me when I travel
or when I lie down
to rest;

\par }{\Q you are aware
of everything I do.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Certainly
my tongue
does not
frame
a word
\par }{\Q without you, O
{\ND{Lord}}, being thoroughly aware of it.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}You squeeze
me in from
behind
and in front;
\par }{\Q you place
your hand
on me.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Your knowledge
is beyond
my comprehension;
\par }{\Q it is so far beyond me,
I am unable
to fathom it.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Where
can I go
to escape your spirit?
\par }{\Q Where
can I flee to escape
your presence?
\par }{\Q \VS{8}If
I were to ascend
to heaven,
you would be there.
\par }{\Q If
I were to sprawl out
in Sheol,
there you would be.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}If I were to fly
away on the wings
of the dawn,
\par }{\Q and settle
down on the other side
of the sea,
\par }{\Q \VS{10}even
there
your hand
would guide
me,
\par }{\Q your right hand
would grab hold of me.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}If I were to say,
“Certainly
the darkness
will cover
me,

\par }{\Q and the light
will turn
to night all around me,”
\par }{\Q \VS{12}even
the darkness
is not
too dark
for you to see,

\par }{\Q and the night
is as bright as
day;
\par }{\Q darkness
and light are the same to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Certainly
you
made
my mind
and heart;
\par }{\Q you wove
me together in my mother’s
womb.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}I will give you thanks
because
your deeds
are awesome
and amazing.
\par }{\Q You knew
me thoroughly;
\par }{\Q \VS{15}my bones were not
hidden
from
you,
\par }{\Q when I was made
in secret
\par }{\Q and sewed
together in the depths
of the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Your eyes
saw
me when I was inside the womb.
\par }{\Q All
the days
ordained
for me
\par }{\Q were recorded
in your scroll
\par }{\Q before one of them came into existence.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}How
difficult it is for me to fathom
your thoughts
about me, O God!

\par }{\Q How
vast is their sum total!
\par }{\Q \VS{18}If I tried to count
them,
\par }{\Q they would outnumber the grains
of sand.
\par }{\Q Even if I finished counting
them,
\par }{\Q I would still
have to contend with you.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}If
only
you would kill the wicked,
O God!
\par }{\Q Get away
from
me, you violent
men!
\par }{\Q \VS{20}They rebel
against you and act
deceitfully;
\par }{\Q your enemies
lie.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}O
{\ND{Lord}}, do I not
hate
those who hate
you,
\par }{\Q and despise
those who oppose you?
\par }{\Q \VS{22}I absolutely
hate
them,
\par }{\Q they have become
my enemies!
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Examine
me, and probe
my thoughts!

\par }{\Q Test
me, and know
my concerns!
\par }{\Q \VS{24}See
if
there is any idolatrous tendency
in me,
\par }{\Q and lead
me in the reliable ancient
path!

{\ND{Lord}}, rescue
